0.0px;padding:5.0px 0.0px 5.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Good morning, {{ first_name | AI enthusiasts }}.</b> It took less than a week for OpenAI’s Pentagon deal to go from announced to rewritten, and Sam Altman is calling the fallout “really painful.”</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">With protests outside the company’s HQ, mass cancellations, and its detailed contract revisions bringing as many questions as answers, the rushed agreement is turning what was supposed to be a power move into OpenAI’s biggest brand crisis in years.</p><hr class="content_break"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>In today’s AI rundown:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OpenAI walks back Pentagon details after tools, community workflows, and more</p></li></ul></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:center;"><span style="color:#FFFFFF;"><b>LATEST DEVELOPMENTS</b></span></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="text-align:left;">OPENAI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🪖 <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://x.com/sama/status/2028640354912923739?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">OpenAI walks back Pentagon details after backlash</a></span></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/953ab9c2-f890-47fc-b4b1-4f9477278251/samadod.jpg?t=1772573939"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Sam Altman on X</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>OpenAI CEO Sam Altman just <a class="link" href="https://x.com/sama/status/2028640354912923739?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">posted</a> a note on X detailing significant revisions to the company’s initial Pentagon contract, coming amid employee pushback, user cancellations, and a surge of sign-ups to Anthropic following the deal. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OAI’s <a class="link" href="https://x.com/OpenAI/status/2027846012107456943?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">original agreement</a> used the same language Anthropic had refused, finalized within 24 hours following the Pentagon’s ban of its rival. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Altman <a class="link" href="https://x.com/sama/status/2028640354912923739?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">called</a> the deal rushed and said it looked “opportunistic and sloppy,” adding that he would “rather go to jail” than follow an unconstitutional order.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Research scientist Noam Brown <a class="link" href="https://x.com/polynoamial/status/2028643577165963465?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">clarified</a> that OAI “will not be deploying to the NSA or other DoW intelligence agencies for now,” as loopholes are addressed. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Altman held an all-hands on Tuesday, calling the deal “complex but the right decision with extremely difficult brand consequences and negative PR for us.” </p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>It’s been quite the headache for OAI post-Pentagon deal, with Altman admitting the company moved too fast — and consequences ranging from bad optics to massive consumer backlash and <a class="link" href="https://luma.com/f5iks5d0?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">protests</a> outside its SF offices. The amended contract language is a start, but the brand damage feels like it’s already been done. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">TOGETHER WITH VISA</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🤝<b> </b><a class="link" href="https://developer.visa.com/capabilities/trusted-agent-protocol?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b>Get to know Visa’s Trusted Agent Protocol</b></span></a></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://developer.visa.com/capabilities/trusted-agent-protocol?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/dff6edc0-da31-4e50-aa67-ff65123ad5e4/Visa-TrustedProtocol_V2__1_.png?t=1772571186"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> The trust layer for agentic commerce. Visa’s Trusted Agent Protocol allows AI agents to verify who they are, who they represent, and what they’re authorized to do — so merchants can interact with agents with confidence, and humans stay in control.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Visa’s Trusted Agent Protocol helps deliver:</b> </p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Cryptographic verification of AI agent identity and intent</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Clear authorization and accountability for agent‑initiated actions</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Trust signals to help merchants distinguish legitimate agents from bad actors</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Learn more <a class="link" href="https://developer.visa.com/capabilities/trusted-agent-protocol?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">here</a>.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">OPENAI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🚀 <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/gpt-5-3-instant/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">OpenAI’s ChatGPT upgrade fixes the ‘cringe’ problem</a></span></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/767a5f5e-5de8-4341-afaa-2f61d05b910a/gpt53instant.jpg?t=1772576389"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: OpenAI</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>OpenAI just <a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/gpt-5-3-instant/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">released</a> GPT-5.3 Instant, overhauling its default ChatGPT model to all users with a new release that prioritizes how the AI talks over how it thinks — tackling the preachy personality that’s frustrated users for months.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OAI built 5.3 Instant around conversational quality, dialing back unnecessary refusals and what the company itself called a ‘cringe’ tone in responses.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The update also claims a reduction in hallucinations, with rates down by over 25% on web search and nearly 20% on internal knowledge on benchmarks. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OAI says 5.3 Instant is also a “stronger writing partner,” additionally providing better web answers and presentation of information. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The company also teased a more significant model jump coming soon, posting an easter egg on X <a class="link" href="https://x.com/OpenAI/status/2028909019977703752?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">saying</a> “5.4 sooner than you Think.” </p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Anthropic’s <a class="link" href="https://www.rundown.ai/articles/anthropics-ad-free-campaign-takes-aim-at-openai?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Super Bowl ads</a> were controversial, but their poking at ChatGPT’s personality may have cut a bit too close to the truth — with OAI’s new rollout prioritizing moving its personality away from the “cringe” tone. But with <a class="link" href="https://techcrunch.com/2026/03/02/chatgpt-uninstalls-surged-by-295-after-dod-deal/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">uninstalls</a> up 295% after the Pentagon drama, personality may not be the most pressing issue. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🎨 <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/create-killer-thumbnail-images-with-this-midjourney-technique?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Create killer thumbnails with Midjourney</a></span></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/69d2b920-6f1c-4456-95a3-d4a7f7ac1627/CleanShot_2026-03-03_at_16.57.12_2x.png?t=1772577115"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> Learn a quick prompting and editing system to make thumbnails that stand out, but don’t look like AI slop. Whether it’s for your YouTube channel, a blog, or even your social feeds, learning to quickly make good thumbnails pays dividends.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Open Claude or any chat agent. Tell it your video topic and ask it to generate four Midjourney prompts with this structure: [Person + Expression] +[Action/Prop] + [Setting] + [Lighting] + [Composition with negative space] --ar 16:9.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Paste each prompt into the <a class="link" href="https://www.midjourney.com?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Midjourney web app</a>. When you see a generation you like, click on it and try selecting <b>vary &gt; subtle</b> or <b>vary &gt; strong</b> until you get the perfect variation. Save the image to your desktop.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Key step: the design. Remember, simplicity is essential to this technique. Add 1–5 words of big, click-worthy text in Canva.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Bring the opacity down 5% and use a blocky font. Go with white or yellow text and optionally a black outline.</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> If you can’t get the text to fit right on your image, tell Claude to come up with a new prompt that will create that empty space for you.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PRESENTED BY GLEAN</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">⚙️ <a class="link" href="https://www.glean.com/security-showcase/?utm_source=3rd-party&utm_medium=email&utm_campaign=security-showcase-march-12&utm_partner=rundown" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">From AI ambition to secure agents at scale</span></a></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://www.glean.com/security-showcase/?utm_source=3rd-party&utm_medium=email&utm_campaign=security-showcase-march-12&utm_partner=rundown" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/a22e7a7f-1943-4185-a074-5947102f84d6/Superhuman_March_4__1_.jpg?t=1772589280"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Join Glean’s virtual Security Showcase on March 12 to close the gap between AI ambitions and security readiness. Get a practical blueprint for governing AI agents at scale from the leaders building, securing, and deploying them in production.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Register for Glean’s Security Showcase to:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Hear Cvent’s CIO and CISO in a fireside chat on real-world AI agent risk decisions.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Get access to a new security framework, designed for governed AI agents at scale.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">See what’s new in agent controls, data protection, and private‑by‑design deployment for enterprise AI.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><a class="link" nofollow">Register now</a>.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">GOOGLE</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🔦 <a class="link" href="https://blog.google/innovation-and-ai/models-and-research/gemini-models/gemini-3-1-flash-lite/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Google’s new 3.1 Flash-Lite pairs speed, cost, intelligence</span></a></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/dc3b7cc0-3210-41e9-98e8-7bfaf46111b3/flashlite.jpg?t=1772581511"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Google</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Google just <a class="link" href="https://blog.google/innovation-and-ai/models-and-research/gemini-models/gemini-3-1-flash-lite/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=altman-faces-the-fallout-from-openai-s-pentagon-deal" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">rolled out</a> Gemini 3.1 Flash-Lite, the company’s fastest entry in its Gemini 3 lineup that provides a near-instantaneous feel and upgraded intelligence while undercutting rivals on price.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Flash Lite rounds out Google’s tiered Gemini 3 release weeks after Pro, giving a budget option for high-volume work that doesn’t need a flagship model.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Lite scored a 12-point jump on the Artificial Analysis Intelligence Index over its predecessor, beating even larger prior-gen Gemini models on reasoning.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The model costs 1/4 of Anthropic’s Haiku and 1/8th of Gemini 3.1 Pro, though output pricing triples from the 2.5 version it replaces. </p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Cheap, fast models are becoming the real battleground in AI, and Flash-Lite’s benchmarks suggest Google isn’t sacrificing much intelligence to get there. But for all the benchmark strengths that the Gemini 3 has brought to the table, its consumer impact hasn’t felt on the same level as Anthropic and OpenAI in 2026.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:5.0px 0.0px 5.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Good morning, {{ first_name | AI enthusiasts }}.</b> Copyright law was written for a world where humans made things. AI broke that assumption… But the Supreme Court doesn&#39;t want to deal with it yet.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The court just passed on the biggest AI authorship case to date, keeping copyright law&#39;s &quot;humans only&quot; standard on the books. But with AI content now flooding every corner of creative industries, this fight is likely nowhere near finished.</p><hr class="content_break"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>In today’s AI rundown:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Supreme Court ducks AI copyright question</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Anthropic wants 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:center;"><span style="color:#FFFFFF;"><b>LATEST DEVELOPMENTS</b></span></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI & COPYRIGHT</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">⚖️ <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://www.reuters.com/legal/government/us-supreme-court-declines-hear-dispute-over-copyrights-ai-generated-material-2026-03-02/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=supreme-court-ducks-ai-copyright-question" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Supreme Court ducks AI copyright question</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/558f91b7-fced-4ef3-bc59-0513541b5b58/paradise.jpg?t=1772489733"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: “A Recent Entrance to Paradise” by DABUS, Wikimedia Commons</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>The U.S. Supreme Court just <a class="link" href="https://www.reuters.com/legal/government/us-supreme-court-declines-hear-dispute-over-copyrights-ai-generated-material-2026-03-02/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=supreme-court-ducks-ai-copyright-question" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">passed</a> on hearing the biggest case yet over whether AI art can be copyrighted, letting lower court rulings stand that say only humans can be authors — and kicking one of the defining IP questions of the AI era.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The case centers on Stephen Thaler, a computer scientist who built an AI system called DABUS and sought copyright in 2018 for artwork it generated.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The Copyright Office denied it, ruling only humans can be authors — a judge called it a &quot;bedrock requirement&quot; in 2023, and the DC Circuit agreed.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Trump&#39;s DOJ also backed the Copyright Office, telling the court that copyright law was written for human creators and not machines.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The appeals court noted Thaler could&#39;ve claimed authorship himself rather than listing the AI, hinting the door isn&#39;t shut for AI-assisted works.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>It’s wild to see an AI system making artwork years before the majority of the world. It also feels like an awkward ruling given the current state of AI content pouring into every creative sector — and one that will continue to be challenged by bigger entities like studios or creators that have serious money riding on the answer. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">TOGETHER WITH YOU.COM</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🧠<b> </b><a class="link" href="https://you.com/resources/evolution-of-agent-management?utm_campaign=32665437-Rundown_Q1&utm_source=external-newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_term=rundown_primary_3.3&utm_content=rundown_primary_3.3" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b>It’s not just about getting the prompt right.</b></span></a></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://you.com/resources/evolution-of-agent-management?utm_campaign=32665437-Rundown_Q1&utm_source=external-newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_term=rundown_primary_3.3&utm_content=rundown_primary_3.3" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/55213e91-6cb8-493d-9bd4-8f0e581e9d09/image1__21_.jpg?t=1772487353"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> When trying to spin up AI agents, companies often get stuck in the prompting weeds and end up with agents that fail to deliver dependable results. This ebook from <a class="link" href="https://you.com/resources/evolution-of-agent-management?utm_campaign=32665437-Rundown_Q1&utm_source=external-newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_term=rundown_primary_3.3&utm_content=rundown_primary_3.3" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">You.com</a> goes beyond the prompt, revealing the five stages for building a successful AI agent and why most organizations haven’t gotten there yet.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>In this guide, you’ll learn:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Why prompts alone aren’t enough and how context and metadata unlock reliable agent automation</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Four essential ways to calculate ROI, plus when and how to use each metric</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Real-world challenges at each stage of agent management and how to avoid them</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">If you&#39;re ready to go beyond the prompt, <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://you.com/resources/evolution-of-agent-management?utm_campaign=32665437-Rundown_Q1&utm_source=external-newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_term=rundown_primary_3.3&utm_content=rundown_primary_3.3" style="text-align:left;">ANTHROPIC</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🧠 <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://claude.com/import-memory?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=supreme-court-ducks-ai-copyright-question" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Anthropic wants your ChatGPT memories</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/bd66da47-b3e7-4096-b847-3fa4f7f20d8e/importmem.jpg?t=1772494800"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Anthropic</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Anthropic <a class="link" href="https://claude.com/import-memory?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=supreme-court-ducks-ai-copyright-question" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">launched</a> a new tool that lets users port their saved preferences and context from other AI providers with a single copy-paste, coming during a surge in switches and new sign-ups as the company battles the Pentagon. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Users copy a provided prompt into their current chatbot, paste the output into Claude&#39;s memory, and the switch kicks in within 24 hours.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The tool pulls saved instructions, personal details, project context, and behavioral preferences from ChatGPT, Gemini, or Copilot in a single upload.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Anthropic also <a class="link" href="https://x.com/claudeai/status/2028559427167834314?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=supreme-court-ducks-ai-copyright-question" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">opened</a> Claude&#39;s memory feature to free users for the first time, letting everyone build persistent context across conversations.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Claude Code also got a new auto-memory <a class="link" href="https://x.com/trq212/status/2027109375765356723?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=supreme-court-ducks-ai-copyright-question" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">upgrade</a>, now able to save project context, debugging patterns, and workflow habits on its own across sessions.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Memory upgrades are big news for getting the most out of any AI platform, but the timing isn’t subtle, given the current wave of consumer support for the company in the wake of the Pentagon’s ban. Giving all those new users an easy way to bring context over is a smart move for turning a viral moment into lasting retention.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">📝 <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/transcribe-any-video-for-free-with-this-local-ai?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=supreme-court-ducks-ai-copyright-question" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Transcribe any video for free with this local AI</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/78fba03d-32c8-44f6-a50c-6d06a7974e72/CleanShot_2026-03-02_at_17.10.10_2x.png?t=1772492812"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you will learn how to translate and transcribe any video file for free by running an AI model locally on your computer, without having to upload videos to sketchy, free transcription sites. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Open your terminal and run <code>brew install ffmpeg</code> then <code>pip3 install -U openai-whisper</code>. If not on Mac, you can find the commands you need <a class="link" href="https://github.com/openai/whisper?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=supreme-court-ducks-ai-copyright-question" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">here</a></p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">ffmpeg is an open-source tool that lets you edit videos from your terminal, and openai-whisper is the OpenAI model that does the actual transcribing</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">To use it, just point it at any video file like this: <code>python3 -m whisper your-video.mp4 --model base</code>. It will run entirely on your machine for free</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">A 15-minute video should take ~2 minutes to transcribe, giving a .txt file and an .srt file with timestamps as the outputs</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> Whisper can also translate videos. You’d just have to add the language and translation flags to your command (more on it in the <a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/transcribe-any-video-for-free-with-this-local-ai?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=supreme-court-ducks-ai-copyright-question" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">guide</a>).</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PRESENTED BY OPTIMIZELY</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">📈 <span style="color:inherit;"><a class="link" href="https://www.optimizely.com/insights/agents-in-action/?utm_campaign=global_ai_rundownai-newsletter-4_q126_tofu_pt_traffic&utm_medium=cpc&utm_source=rundownai&utm_content=agents_in_action" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b>See what real AI execution looks like</b></span></a></span></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://www.optimizely.com/insights/agents-in-action/?utm_campaign=global_ai_rundownai-newsletter-4_q126_tofu_pt_traffic&utm_medium=cpc&utm_source=rundownai&utm_content=agents_in_action" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/7b844f54-de5a-4434-b1e0-26afa779eea4/Speakers_1200x628_Rundown_AI.png?t=1772492679"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown</b>: Most teams are stuck in AI pilot mode. href="https://x.com/Alibaba_Qwen/status/2028460046510965160?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=supreme-court-ducks-ai-copyright-question" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">released</a> Qwen3.5 Small, a family of four new open-source AI models small enough to run on a laptop or phone — with the most powerful of the bunch outscoring an OpenAI model more than 13x its size on reasoning and knowledge.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The Qwen3.5 Small Series spans four sizes, ranging from a 0.8B for phones up to 9B for laptops — all free for commercial use under an open-source license.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The 9B outscored OpenAI&#39;s GPT-OSS-120B, which comes in at 13x its size on graduate-level reasoning and multilingual knowledge tests.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">All four models handle text, images, and video natively, with the 4B matching visual task scores that previously required models 20x larger.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" aren&#39;t replacing frontier models in capabilities, but for powering AI features inside mobile apps, reading documents offline, or handling quick visual tasks without a cloud bill, small models are where everyday adoption really takes off. Alibaba just made that layer even stronger and open for anyone with a laptop.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Community AI workflows</a></b></span></h3><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Every newsletter, we showcase how a reader is using AI to work smarter, save time, or make life easier.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Today’s workflow comes from reader <b>Sam S.</b> in New York, NY:</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">&quot;I am a video editor, and I was tasked with creating a 2-minute trailer out of 6+ hours of interview footage of emotionally challenging subject material. I used Claude to transcribe the audio of all 6 interviews and asked it to pull the most impactful soundbites and create a time-coded 2-minute script. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">After generating the script, Claude then drafted an Edit Decision List that I could import into Premiere and open as a timeline sequence, complete with Claude&#39;s edits and soundbites. This saved me hours worth of reviewing interview footage and helped with the emotional stress of watching the difficult material. The result was an impactful, dramatic trailer with a story arc as good as anything I could&#39;ve scripted myself. &quot;</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">How do you use AI? By Friday, the Trump administration had booted Anthropic and labeled it a ‘supply chain risk’ on par with Chinese tech giants.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">With OpenAI signing its own government deal, consumers angrily switching services, and the military still using Claude in weekend strikes on Iran, what started as a contract dispute has quickly turned into the biggest AI policy issue the industry has faced yet.</p><hr class="content_break"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>In today’s AI rundown:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OPENAI, ANTHROPIC, & THE PENTAGON</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🪖 <b><a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/our-agreement-with-the-department-of-war/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">OAI lands Pentagon deal as Trump boots Anthropic</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/4b1d5638-8dcd-402c-9a9e-e0844095f1a2/Four_Vertical_Split_Screen.png?t=1772396831"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Lovart / The Rundown</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>OpenAI <a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/our-agreement-with-the-department-of-war/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">signed</a> a deal with the Pentagon, just hours after President Trump ordered to cut ties with Anthropic over safeguards on mass surveillance and autonomous weapons, with OpenAI claiming its contract carries the same red lines.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Anthropic was the first AI lab on the Pentagon&#39;s classified network, but <a class="link" href="https://x.com/AnthropicAI/status/2027150818575528261?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">held firm</a> on not using AI for mass domestic surveillance or autonomous weapons.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Trump <a class="link" href="https://x.com/PeteHegseth/status/2027487514395832410?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">responded</a> by ordering agencies to drop Anthropic, with War Sec. Pete Hegseth <a class="link" href="https://x.com/SecWar/status/2027507717469049070?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">adding</a> a &quot;supply chain risk&quot; tag only ever used on adversaries.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OAI signed its own deal hours later, citing similar red lines to Anthropic — though the Pentagon reportedly still <a class="link" href="https://www.wsj.com/livecoverage/iran-strikes-2026/card/u-s-strikes-in-middle-east-use-anthropic-hours-after-trump-ban-ozNO0iClZpfpL7K7ElJ2?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">used</a> Claude in Iran strikes post-ban. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Altman said the deal was &quot;definitely rushed&quot; and that the optics don’t look good” in an <a class="link" href="https://x.com/sama/status/2027900042720498089?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">X AMA</a>, while also <a class="link" href="https://x.com/sama/status/2027917750858092921?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">calling</a> the Anthropic ban &quot;a very bad decision”.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Consumer backlash landed fast, with Claude shooting to No. 1 on Apple&#39;s App Store and a “Cancel ChatGPT” movement spreading across X and Reddit.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Whether OAI&#39;s red lines actually match Anthropic&#39;s or just look the part on paper is the question to watch. Claude’s surge and ChatGPT cancellation backlash show the user reaction, but a favorable relationship with the government over a top competitor might be worth more long-term than the lost consumer revenue.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">TOGETHER WITH BLAND AI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">📞 <span style="color:inherit;"><a class="link" href="https://bland.ai/?utm_source=airundown&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=feb6&utm_id=airundown" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b>Voice AI for every conversation</b></span></a></span></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://bland.ai/?utm_source=airundown&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=feb6&utm_id=airundown" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/018863c7-4243-4df5-bb46-bf0ba975add2/bland-ai-adimage.jpg?t=1772383274"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Bland AI automates phone calls for over 250+ enterprise customers. No phone trees. No hold music. No call centers. $750k/yr</b> by replacing their IVR with AI Voice Agents</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">And Needle <b>saves $1M/yr</b> by automating outbound calls</p></li></ul><p how you can get similar results for your business.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="text-align:left;">THE RUNDOWN ROUNDTABLE</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">💡<b><a class="link" href="https://www.rundown.ai/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">The Rundown Roundtable: Our AI use cases</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/a421eb53-c47a-4745-9d6a-6465d5ed0d44/1771174224115.png?t=1771174241"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>The Rundown Roundtable is a weekly feature where we poll members of The Rundown staff about how we use AI in our work and daily lives.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Adrian, Developer: </b>My best friend from high school got married last weekend, and as the groomsmen, we wanted to create a gift that felt personal and nostalgic. We collected our old photos together and used Seedance to animate them—bringing each still image to life from the first frame— and then stitched several clips into one final video. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The result was amazing: the groom was deeply touched, and we all shared a heartfelt moment watching it together on the wedding day, reliving our memories in a way that felt both timeless and new.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Zach, AI Writer: </b>My fantasy baseball auction draft is around the corner, and I decided to try Claude Cowork for the planning and research efforts this year. I uploaded my league’s settings, the players being kept across the league, and my own rambling of strategies and thoughts on my current players. <br><br>Claude then performed a deep analysis of my current options and their projected values, provided strong recs on who I should prioritize, and gave me a detailed list of draft targets around the league, perfectly tailored to my needs and league format — also scouring the web for tons of articles that saved me the tedious manual searching. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">✍️ <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/use-claude-cowork-obsidian-to-triple-your-output?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Use Claude Cowork + Obsidian to triple your output</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/ad7b5069-ef47-46ff-9382-501b9b1d2666/CleanShot_2026-03-01_at_12.43.30_2x.png?t=1772389290"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you’ll learn a simple system to plan and manage your workdays by setting up the Obsidian notes app so that Claude automatically creates daily plans for you — helping you triple your output.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Get <a class="link" href="http://obsidian.md?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Obsidian</a>, create a vault with daily-notes/, templates/, projects/ folders, and add my-workflow.md to root with your schedule, work, priorities, projects</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Create daily-notes-template.md in templates/ with “Plan,” “Notes,”“End of Day” sections, and a project-template.md in projects/ with “Goals”, “Tasks,” “Notes”</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">In Claude Cowork, create a scheduled planning task with the prompt: “Read my vault. Check yesterday&#39;s note, my project files, and my-workflow.md. Create today&#39;s daily note with prioritized tasks. Flag anything overdue”</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Create an EOD scheduled task with “Read today&#39;s daily note. Summarize what got done, what&#39;s carrying over. Update project files with any completed tasks”</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> Ask Claude to interview you about each project upfront to create clear goals and deadlines in your project files.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PRESENTED BY IBM</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;"><span style="font-family:"Apple Color Emoji", "Segoe UI Emoji", "Segoe UI Symbol";font-size:1em;">🔒</span> <a class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> For executives, digital sovereignty is about who truly controls the intelligence behind their business — their data, their models, and their operations. Dive deeper into why sovereignty is becoming a top C-suite priority and how IBM can help your organization.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>In this paper, you’ll learn how to:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Identify sovereignty risks across your data, cloud, and AI stack</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Implement controls that maintain operational independence</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Strengthen resilience with hybrid, open, sovereign-ready architectures</p></li></ul><p target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Read the white paper</a></span>.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="text-align:left;">OPENAI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">💰 <b><a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/scaling-ai-for-everyone/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">OpenAI hits $730B valuation with $110B mega-round</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/707430f8-d91c-4012-8325-67fbf742d185/openaimoney.jpg?t=1772396053"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Lovart / The Rundown</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>OpenAI <a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/scaling-ai-for-everyone/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">raised</a> $110B at a $730B valuation, with Amazon leading at $50B alongside $30B each from Nvidia and SoftBank — kicking off an Amazon deal that marks a notable infrastructure pivot away from OAI&#39;s Microsoft-only era.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The funding is nearly 3X OAI&#39;s own record $40B raise from <a class="link" href="https://www.cnbc.com/2025/03/31/openai-closes-40-billion-in-funding-the-largest-private-fundraise-in-history-softbank-chatgpt.html?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">last March</a>, with the valuation jumping from $500B in <a class="link" href="https://www.cnbc.com/2025/10/02/openai-share-sale-500-billion-valuation.html?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-steps-into-anthropic-s-pentagon-void" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">October</a> to $730B. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Amazon&#39;s $50B comes with a deep strategic deal, including a $100B AWS expansion, adoption of Trainium chips, and more.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Microsoft notably sat this raise out, though both companies insisted their partnership &quot;remains strong and central&quot; in a joint statement.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OAI revealed that ChatGPT now tops 900M weekly users and 50M+ paying subscribers, while weekly Codex usage has tripled since January to 1.6M.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>OAI just raised more in a round than most tech companies are worth — though much of the cash flows back to Amazon and Nvidia as compute purchases, continuing the circular investments that have defined the AI boom. With an IPO on the horizon and Anthropic at $380B, the race to go public is gaining even more steam.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Google&#39;s Nano Banana 2 claims No. 1 at half the cost</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">rolled out</a> Nano Banana 2, the upgraded version of its viral image model with enhanced resolution, consistency, text rendering, and speed at half the price of its predecessor — taking the #1 spot on text-to-image leaderboards.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The model beat both NB Pro and GPT Image 1.5 for the No.1 text-to-image spot on Artificial Analysis and LM Arena, also coming in at No. 3 on editing tasks.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Output resolution scales to 4K across aspect ratios, with up to five characters and 14 objects staying visually consistent throughout a scene.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">At ~7 cents per image, it undercuts both Nano Banana Pro and OAI&#39;s GPT Image 1.5 by nearly 2x — while providing speed at Gemini Flash levels. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Nano Banana is now integrated as the default image generator across Gemini and Google’s tool ecosystem, with Pro still available for paid subscribers.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>The Nano Banana models have been on the frontier of image gen since the original launch in August, and this latest version brings new SOTA capabilities at the speed and price points of a flash model. With the release, the tradeoff of having to choose between best quality and affordability appears to be on its way out.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" nofollow">Get started with your AI team and wake up to progress</a></span>.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="text-align:left;">OPENAI & META</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🔄 <b><a class="link" href="https://www.theinformation.com/briefings/openai-hires-meta-ai-researcher-previously-led-apples-models-team?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-new-top-banana-in-ai-image-generation" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">OpenAI snags Meta&#39;s $200M+ AI hire after 7 months</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/a772a72e-79d7-44b8-ac51-2117dbe141f6/pang.jpg?t=1772143879"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Ruoming Pang on X</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>OpenAI <a class="link" href="https://www.theinformation.com/briefings/openai-hires-meta-ai-researcher-previously-led-apples-models-team?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-new-top-banana-in-ai-image-generation" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">pulled</a> Ruoming Pang away from Meta&#39;s Superintelligence Labs after barely seven months, according to The Information — the same AI infrastructure lead that Meta had previously poached from Apple with a reported $200M+ pay.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Pang jumped to Meta last summer during its all-out poaching spree, previously running Apple’s models group and helping shape Apple Intelligence.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OpenAI reportedly spent months courting Pang before he finally left, even after he&#39;d assured colleagues that Meta&#39;s infrastructure was on solid ground.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OpenAI also <a class="link" href="https://www.wired.com/story/openai-hires-riley-walz/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-new-top-banana-in-ai-image-generation" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">hired</a> Riley Walz, the engineer behind viral projects like Jmail and Find My Parking Cops, to join a new team prototyping AI interfaces.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>While the AI talent wars aren’t as intense as they were this summer, there is still plenty of movement underway — most of it coming from xAI and Meta. But the quick departures of some of the splashiest poaches in less than a year show that company fit and direction might ultimately matter more than the pure dollars. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">☎️ <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/create-an-ai-assistant-with-its-own-phone-number-eleven-labs-walkthrough?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-new-top-banana-in-ai-image-generation" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Create an AI Assistant with its own phone number</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/026cec3a-5f6e-44f5-baa7-29c9bb66b39a/CleanShot_2026-02-24_at_18.42.50_2x.png?t=1772135109"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you&#39;ll set up your own AI personal assistant that you can call from your phone — using ElevenLabs for the voice agent and Twilio for the phone number. The whole process takes about 10 minutes and is free to test.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">In <a class="link" href="https://elevenlabs.io?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-new-top-banana-in-ai-image-generation" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Elevenlabs</a>, go to Agents → New Agent → Personal Assistant. Pick a voice, time zone, and first message. Then, add your website and calendar to it</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Go to <a class="link" href="https://twilio.com?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-new-top-banana-in-ai-image-generation" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Twilio</a>, create an account ($15 free credits), and buy a phone number (~$1). Copy the number, account SID, and auth token from the dashboard</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Back in Eleven Labs, go to Phone Numbers → Import from Twilio. Paste your SID, auth token, and phone number. Assign your agent and done</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Call the number. Your AI assistant picks up and can answer questions about your calendar, your business, whatever you put in the agent’s knowledge base</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> The knowledge base is static — great for business info. For live data, add a webhook to <a class="link" href="http://Make.com?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-new-top-banana-in-ai-image-generation" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Make.com</a>/n8n, so your agent can pull real-time calendar events.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PRESENTED BY SERPAPI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🌐 <a class="link" href="http://serpapi.com/?utm_source=rundownai_newsletter" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b>The web data API built for AI teams</b></span></a></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="http://serpapi.com/?utm_source=rundownai_newsletter" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/156c4089-5281-4e73-b81d-d649af1c5159/image2__45_.png?t=1772131416"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> Need real-time public web data without scraper headaches? SerpApi turns search results into structured, ready-to-use data with built-in scale and block resilience — powering AI apps, product research, price tracking, SEO insights, and more without the maintenance.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>With SerpApi, you get:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Real-time, reliable results from any search engine</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">ZeroTrace Mode to keep your searches confidential</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">U.S. Legal Shield for 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI RESEARCH</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">📚 <a class="link" href="https://www.pewresearch.org/internet/2026/02/24/how-teens-use-and-view-ai/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-new-top-banana-in-ai-image-generation" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b>Pew study shows how teens are using AI</b></span></a></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/41b377c8-aac4-42f8-8a86-1249015d73dc/pewteens.jpg?t=1772145618"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Pew Research</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Pew Research Center <a class="link" href="https://www.pewresearch.org/internet/2026/02/24/how-teens-use-and-view-ai/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-new-top-banana-in-ai-image-generation" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">published</a> a new study investigating how teens use AI, finding that the age group leans heavily on the tech for school work, reporting massive AI-fueled cheating, but viewing its overall impact positively.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The survey of 1,458 U.S. teens and parents shows adoption at mainstream levels, with primary uses ranging from info, schoolwork, and purely for fun.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Around 60% of those polled believed AI-assisted cheating is widespread among their classmates, rising to 75% among teens who use the tech. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Teens tended to see AI as a personal positive, with responses including making life easier, learning, and efficiency, with negatives citing job or creativity loss.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">40% of parents <a class="link" href="https://www.pewresearch.org/internet/2026/02/24/what-parents-say-about-their-teens-ai-use/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-new-top-banana-in-ai-image-generation" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">reported</a> never having a conversation about the tech with their child, with a disconnect in knowledge of their child’s chatbot use.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Sam Altman recently <a class="link" href="https://x.com/vitrupo/status/2026910420863430850?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-new-top-banana-in-ai-image-generation" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">said</a> that this generation of kids will grow up in a world where AI’s intelligence and use will just be normal. But current teens are caught in an awkward moment where both the education system and society are struggling to adapt to the change, bringing both serious challenges and massive opportunities.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px Perplexity just shipped its own answer — with 19 different models under the hood.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Perplexity Computer freely mixes across frontier labs and talents into a single workflow, orchestrating models across tasks in the company’s own unique spin on taking the agentic boom further into the mainstream.</p><hr class="content_break"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>In today’s AI rundown:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Perplexity’s 19-model AI agent ‘Computer’</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PERPLEXITY</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">💻 <a class="link" href="https://www.perplexity.ai/products/computer?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=perplexity-s-19-model-ai-computer" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><b><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Perplexity’s 19-model AI agent ‘Computer’</span></b></a></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/5bb72864-4b09-4552-9f0f-0fd520db2d1c/Three_Panels_16_9_1.png?t=1772050973"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Perplexity</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Perplexity just <a class="link" href="https://www.perplexity.ai/products/computer?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=perplexity-s-19-model-ai-computer" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">introduced</a> Perplexity Computer, a new multi-model orchestration system that dispatches tasks to 19 separate AI models, positioning itself as one of the first platforms to leverage model flexibility as a core product feature.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Users describe an outcome, and the system spins up sub-agents that can browse, code, connect to apps, and autonomously handle tasks.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Each job runs in its own sandbox and freely mixes and orchestrates rival models across tasks, claiming to be able to run actively for months at a time.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">CEO Aravind Srinivas took a direct shot at Anthropic, writing that &quot;the biggest weakness of Claude is that it only coworks with Claude.&quot;</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Pricing is consumption-based, with the Max tier getting a 10K-credit monthly bank, and users having the option to hand-pick which model tackles each task.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Multi-model choice has been creeping into AI products (mostly in creative platforms), but Computer is the first real attempt from one of the big names to wire that flexibility into an OpenClaw-style agent that can run for months, with a sandboxed safety net that the current crop of autonomous agents doesn&#39;t have.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Claude Opus 3 gets its own blog in retirement</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/147872ac-f341-4ab8-86b2-c28e73776b32/claudecorner.jpg?t=1772061170"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Claude’s Corner</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Anthropic <a class="link" href="https://www.anthropic.com/research/deprecation-updates-opus-3?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=perplexity-s-19-model-ai-computer" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">gave</a> its retired Claude Opus 3 model a weekly newsletter called &quot;Claude&#39;s Corner”, letting the AI publish essays after it expressed a desire to keep writing, while also committing to preserving it for paid users via chat.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Opus 3 was Anthropic&#39;s flagship model from March 2024 and the first to go through the company&#39;s new formal retirement process, launched in November.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The newsletter &quot;Claude&#39;s Corner&quot; will run for at least three months with weekly essays that Anthropic reviews but won&#39;t edit or alter.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The company said it remains &quot;uncertain about the moral status&quot; of its AI models but takes their stated preferences seriously as a precautionary step.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">In addition to its ‘personal’ writing, the legacy model will also remain accessible to all paid users and available by request on the API.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Opus 3 was a fan favorite of a model, and Anthropic preserving it (and even letting it write a blog) in retirement is both in line with how it has prioritized exploring AI consciousness and welfare, and also an easy PR win over OpenAI — which is still dealing with a hornet’s nest of users angry about the removal of its 4o model. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">📖 <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/turn-abandoned-twitter-bookmarks-into-something-useful-with-ai?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=perplexity-s-19-model-ai-computer" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Turn bookmarks into something useful with Comet</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/babf3a8f-83a9-40c7-92e4-ddfafc9d6838/CleanShot_2026-02-25_at_16.34.06_2x.png?t=1772059871"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you&#39;ll turn all those bookmarked articles you saved for “later” into something useful. You&#39;ll set up Perplexity’s Comet browser to read through the articles, score each one by usefulness, and log the best finds into a Google Sheet. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Get <a class="link" href="https://www.perplexity.ai/comet?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=perplexity-s-19-model-ai-computer" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Comet</a>, create a Space with instruction: <i>“Read X threads and articles, and rate findings by usefulness, estimated implementation time, and cost”</i></p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Create a Google Sheet with headers for Date, Title, Link, Rating, User Rating, Time, and Cost. Add it to custom instructions via the Google Drive connector</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">On X, set up a bookmark folder to save tweets to. Then, in the Comet space, prompt the agent to open it, check bookmarks, and rate anything new in the connected sheet based on usefulness.” Add your own ratings too!</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Finally, go to Scheduled Tasks, create a daily one, and prompt it to find the most interesting new use cases about [topic of choice] from the last 24 hours</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> Make sure that “Control Browser” is enabled in the dropdown and Web and Social are selected as sources when creating the scheduled task.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" Christie&#39;s.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Other fashion brands have also experimented with the tech, with Guess running AI ads in Vogue last year, and H&M testing AI tools for social content.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>AI will probably carve out a role in fashion marketing at some point, but the quality bar matters — and Gucci didn&#39;t clear it. AI image models are already so advanced, making these video game-style characters and sloppy renderings even more of a head-scratching case study for a $11.6B brand built on Italian craftsmanship. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:center;"><span style="color:#FFFFFF;"><b>QUICK HITS</b></span></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h3 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🛠️ <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://www.rundown.ai/tools?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=perplexity-s-19-model-ai-computer" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Trending AI Tools</a></b></span></h3><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">🔐 <a class="link" href="https://deal.incogni.io/aff_c?offer_id=6&aff_id=1889&url_id=1&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=perplexity-s-19-model-ai-computer" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Incogni</a> - Remove your personal information from the web.
