style="text-align:left;">ANTHROPIC & THE PENTAGON</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🪖 <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://www.axios.com/2026/02/24/anthropic-pentagon-claude-hegseth-dario?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=pentagon-hits-claude-with-scary-ai-ultimatum" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Pentagon hits Claude with ultimatum over guardrails</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/0b0ba87e-2a89-4352-899d-61e29eeb56ee/HB23rT0XIAECKyz.jpeg?t=1771971896"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Full Metal Jacket / The Rundown</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>The Pentagon and Defense Secretary Pete Hegseth just <a class="link" href="https://www.axios.com/2026/02/24/anthropic-pentagon-claude-hegseth-dario?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=pentagon-hits-claude-with-scary-ai-ultimatum" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">delivered</a> a Friday ultimatum to Anthropic CEO Dario Amodei: remove Claude&#39;s military safeguards, or face contract termination, government blacklisting, and forced compliance.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Amodei has refused to budge on two Claude uses — autonomous weapons without a human in the loop, and bulk surveillance of American citizens.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Axios reports Hegseth gave three choices: Agree, kill the $200M deal with a supply chain risk label, or be forced to comply via the Defense Production Act.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Claude was the first model inside the Pentagon&#39;s classified networks, with xAI’s Grok now <a class="link" href="https://www.axios.com/2026/02/23/ai-defense-department-deal-musk-xai-grok?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=pentagon-hits-claude-with-scary-ai-ultimatum" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">landing</a> a deal after agreeing to “all lawful purposes” use cases.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The Pentagon is also reportedly fast-tracking OpenAI and Google for classified access, giving it additional options if Anthropic walks.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>AI is becoming a pillar of military power, but strong-arming labs into dropping safety limits sets a bleak precedent. If ‘wartime’ legal threats are enough to strip guardrails, the question of who will actually draw the line on dystopian AI uses like autonomous weapons and surveillance quickly gets a very unsettling answer.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">TOGETHER WITH SLACK FROM SALESFORCE</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">👋<b> </b><a class="link" href="https://slack.com/features/slackbot/demo-slackbot?d=701ed00000D87kgAAB&nc=701ed00000D8aHzAAJ&utm_source=therundownai&utm_medium=tp_email&utm_campaign=amer_us_slack-invoice_&utm_content=allsegments_all-strategic-therundown-secondary-slackbotdemo-mar5_701ed00000D87kgAAB_english_demo-slackbot" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b>Learn Slackbot in 2 minutes</b></span></a></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://slack.com/features/slackbot/demo-slackbot?d=701ed00000D87kgAAB&nc=701ed00000D8aHzAAJ&utm_source=therundownai&utm_medium=tp_email&utm_campaign=amer_us_slack-invoice_&utm_content=allsegments_all-strategic-therundown-secondary-slackbotdemo-mar5_701ed00000D87kgAAB_english_demo-slackbot" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/e92deb68-538a-4424-93c1-82948f56b08f/image1__54_.png?t=1771955916"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Slackbot is a context-aware AI agent built directly into Slack — understanding your conversations, files, and workflows to deliver what you need, right when you need it, with zero setup.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Watch this 2-minute demo to see how Slackbot:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Makes your entire workspace searchable (docs, convos, apps)</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Enhances every teammate with role-specific automations</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Learns your project and preferences over time for even smarter outputs</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Synthesizes what you need instantly, respecting permissions and using only what you can already see</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://slack.com/features/slackbot/demo-slackbot?d=701ed00000D87kgAAB&nc=701ed00000D8aHzAAJ&utm_source=therundownai&utm_medium=tp_email&utm_campaign=amer_us_slack-invoice_&utm_content=allsegments_all-strategic-therundown-secondary-slackbotdemo-mar5_701ed00000D87kgAAB_english_demo-slackbot" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Watch now</a></span>.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">STANDARD INTELLIGENCE</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">💻 <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://si.inc/posts/fdm1/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=pentagon-hits-claude-with-scary-ai-ultimatum" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">New AI learns any computer task by watching videos</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/539bfd17-3b3d-418b-844c-871429cec664/standardintell.jpg?t=1771972922"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Standard Intelligence</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Standard Intelligence <a class="link" href="https://si.inc/posts/fdm1/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=pentagon-hits-claude-with-scary-ai-ultimatum" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">introduced</a> FDM-1, a ‘computer action’ model that learns to operate computers by watching video — already showing it can do CAD modeling, find software bugs, and drive a real car through San Francisco.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">FDM-1 is trained on 11M hours of screen footage, 550,000x (!) the largest open dataset, with an AI that reverse-engineers what actions produced each frame.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The model can watch and follow along with nearly two hours of continuous screen activity at once, processing 50x the visual context of existing models.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">FDM-1 Demos range from <a class="link" href="https://x.com/si_pbc/status/2025978967698858020?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=pentagon-hits-claude-with-scary-ai-ultimatum" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">building gears</a> in Blender to <a class="link" href="https://x.com/si_pbc/status/2025978970131607737?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=pentagon-hits-claude-with-scary-ai-ultimatum" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">driving</a> a real car via arrow keys and live data feeds with under an hour of training data.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Language models learned how we write from the internet&#39;s text, and FDM-1 is now trying to learn how we work and operate from the internet&#39;s video. By enabling much more of the world’s video to be ingested as training data with better retention, the ceiling for what computer-use agents can do just jumped dramatically.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🎙️ <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/translate-your-videos-into-any-language-with-ai-full-heygen-tutorial?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=pentagon-hits-claude-with-scary-ai-ultimatum" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Translate your videos into any language with AI</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/dfe3e9a5-fbcc-44fe-95a5-ae178f30a016/CleanShot_2026-02-24_at_17.02.26_2x.png?t=1771971563"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you will learn how to use HeyGen to translate your videos into any language. If you’re running paid or organic video content to an international audience, this is a powerful, easy-to-use way to expand your reach across the globe. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">First, do some research in your Meta/Google ads accounts for your top 3 non-English markets</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">We’re using a free <a class="link" href="https://www.heygen.com/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=pentagon-hits-claude-with-scary-ai-ultimatum" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">HeyGen</a> account, which allows three translations. Keep your video under 3 minutes — a single-speaker talking head format works best</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Click <b>Translate</b> in HeyGen and upload the clip or provide a YT/Google Drive link. Next, choose the required language without changing the default settings</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">In 5–10 minutes, your video will be ready for you to download or share via link</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> If the quality looks low, a paid plan will allow you to export in the original quality.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PRESENTED BY LAMBDA</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;"><b>⚡ </b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://lambda.ai/blog/lambda-and-oumi-partner-for-end-to-end-custom-model-development?utm_source=rundown-ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=2026-02-oumi-partnership&utm_content=main-ad-feb-25" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><b>Build custom AI models in hours, not months</b></a></span></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://lambda.ai/blog/lambda-and-oumi-partner-for-end-to-end-custom-model-development?utm_source=rundown-ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=2026-02-oumi-partnership&utm_content=main-ad-feb-25" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/96b27bc1-f9f3-4e31-b5db-8bd001c4bc7d/image1__55_.png?t=1771956019"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Enterprises stuck on large, closed models are paying more for less control. target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Agentic Workflows Bootcamp pt. 3</a></p></li></ul></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" and Moonshot ran a combined 16M exchanges across thousands of fake accounts to clone Claude’s capabilities into their own models, a scheme it says demands industry-wide action.</p><hr style="text-align:left;">ANTHROPIC</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🕵️ <b><a class="link" href="https://www.anthropic.com/news/detecting-and-preventing-distillation-attacks?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-calls-out-china-s-ai-copycats" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Anthropic catches Chinese labs copying Claude</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/6e40b225-d16c-497a-82ca-f6b0e806cc96/1771888611957.png?t=1771888626"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Lovart / The Rundown </p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Anthropic just <a class="link" href="https://www.anthropic.com/news/detecting-and-preventing-distillation-attacks?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-calls-out-china-s-ai-copycats" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">revealed</a> that DeepSeek, Moonshot, and MiniMax ran coordinated ops to siphon Claude&#39;s capabilities through 16M+ fraudulent exchanges across 24K fake accounts — a threat it says demands immediate industry-wide action.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Anthropic accused the labs of distillation via the conversations, which involves training a weaker system on the outputs from a stronger one. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">MiniMax ran the largest campaign at 13M+ exchanges, and Anthropic caught it mid-operation, spotting the lab shift focus to a new release in under 24 hours.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">DeepSeek had Claude spell out reasoning step-by-step and rewrite politically sensitive queries, generating training data for both logic and censorship.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OAI <a class="link" href="https://finance.yahoo.com/news/openai-accuses-deepseek-distilling-us-213928567.html?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-calls-out-china-s-ai-copycats" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">raised</a> similar concerns with Congress weeks ago, and Anthropic is now pushing for coordinated action from the broader AI industry and government.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Chinese AI has been pulling closer and closer to the frontier — but it’s looking like it may have at least partially been on the backs of the same models they are chasing. But the labs also may find the public low on sympathy, given the industry’s own legal issues and controversies over where their training data comes from. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">TOGETHER WITH TELEPORT</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🤖 <b><a class="link" href="https://fandf.co/4afn32O?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-calls-out-china-s-ai-copycats" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Production-ready identity for AI agents</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://fandf.co/4afn32O?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-calls-out-china-s-ai-copycats" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/eae2e453-6a9c-464d-b42f-af99bd01c865/image1__52_.png?t=1771872501"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>AI agents are moving to production, but legacy IAM can’t secure autonomous actors at scale. Teleport’s Agentic Identity Framework is a standards-driven architecture for running agents across infra with built-in identity, access, and governance.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">What’s new:</p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Short-lived, delegated agent identity</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" href="https://x.com/summeryue0/status/2025774069124399363?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-calls-out-china-s-ai-copycats" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">revealed</a> that her OpenClaw agent went rogue on her inbox, saying it ignored stop commands and started to mass-delete her emails — forcing her to sprint to her Mac mini to kill the process.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Yue said the bot ran fine on a test inbox for weeks, but lost her &quot;confirm before acting&quot; prompt when she gave it access to her much larger real inbox.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Yue called it a &quot;rookie mistake,&quot; saying that &quot;alignment researchers aren&#39;t immune to misalignment&quot;.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Elon Musk piled on, <a class="link" full access to digital lives, so the fact that Meta’s alignment director is having this experience doesn’t bode well for novices (in its current form). The agentic path is still early in being paved, and this is just one of many insane situations set to pop up along the journey.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">💼 <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/build-better-decks-with-ai-works-with-any-tool?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-calls-out-china-s-ai-copycats" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Build better slide decks with AI</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/caa93414-3c75-41de-a73e-7159b60d948a/CleanShot_2026-02-23_at_13.53.22_2x.png?t=1771885598"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you will learn to take raw data and turn it into a presentation-ready slide deck. This works whether you&#39;re starting from a spreadsheet, a meeting transcript, a long document, or just bullet points.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Grab the files you want to start with. This could be a CSV export from Shopify or Google Analytics, a meeting transcript from Zoom, or a scope of work</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Launch Claude, attach the file/doc, and prompt: “I need you to turn these documents into a slide deck outline. Before you start, ask me 5 multiple-choice questions about the purpose, audience, tone, and structure”</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Answer the Qs to get Claude’s outline. Then, go to <a class="link" href="https://gamma.app?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-calls-out-china-s-ai-copycats" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Gamma</a> &gt; Create New &gt; Generate from outline and paste it. Click Continue and check the deck preview</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Finally, click Generate, and Gamma will create a full deck for you that you can edit with AI and export as a PowerPoint or PDF</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> In preview, select “Preserve” and “Concise” options to get the best slide deck.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PRESENTED BY TELY AI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">💬 <b><a class="link" href="https://www.tely.ai/?utm_source=newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_campaign=rundown-jul-25" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Market leaders get leads from ChatGPT and Google</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://www.tely.ai/?utm_source=newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_campaign=rundown-jul-25" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/2ceb94e7-1dd8-4010-bb94-0ea971249303/Run_down_February__1_.png?t=1771874490"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Your buyers are asking, and AI is answering with someone else’s company. Not because you are worse, but because your website doesn’t answer the questions AI looks for. Tely makes Google, ChatGPT, & Claude recommend your business — so when people ask, they find you and reach out.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>With Tely AI, you can:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Get recommended in ChatGPT, Google, Perplexity, and Claude in as little as 1 week</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Fully hands-off: no writers, no agencies, no managing content</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Costs less than hiring freelancers or maintaining a rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Get leads from Google and ChatGPT on autopilot</a></span></span><span style="color:inherit;">.</span></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="heading" style="text-align:left;">OPENAI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">💼 <b><a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/frontier-alliance-partners/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-calls-out-china-s-ai-copycats" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">OpenAI enlists consulting giants for Frontier agents</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/0cf618a8-355d-4726-b9a8-9a8b382ecd09/frontier-alliance.jpg?t=1771888904"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: OpenAI</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>OpenAI just <a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/frontier-alliance-partners/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-calls-out-china-s-ai-copycats" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">announced</a> new multi-year deals with consulting giants McKinsey, BCG, Accenture, and Capgemini as part of the company’s new “Frontier Alliance” enterprise platform push. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OpenAI <a class="link" href="https://www.therundown.ai/p/openai-anthropic-fight-on-the-frontier?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-calls-out-china-s-ai-copycats" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">launched</a> Frontier in early February, a platform giving enterprises the ability to manage AI agents like new hires across existing tech stacks.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">‘Frontier Alliance’ partners will work with OpenAI to help their customers actually integrate AI into their corporate workflows and systems. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The firms are building certified teams that will work alongside OAI&#39;s own engineers, with Accenture already running staff through enterprise AI training.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Building the best AI means nothing if companies can&#39;t figure out where to plug it in, and that gap is exactly what OpenAI and the big consulting firms are looking to close. The irony is that a technology seemingly racing to replace white-collar work is now enlisting the leading consulting firms to get companies AI-integrated.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:center;"><span style="color:#FFFFFF;"><b>QUICK HITS</b></span></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h3 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🛠️ <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://www.rundown.ai/tools?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-calls-out-china-s-ai-copycats" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Trending AI Tools</a></b></span></h3><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">👨‍💻 <a class="link" href="https://link.therundown.ai/d9FwZU?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-calls-out-china-s-ai-copycats" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">HeyGen</a> - Turn ideas into videos in minutes, with no filming required. href="https://www.theinformation.com/articles/inside-openai-team-developing-ai-devices?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=what-openai-and-jony-ive-are-building" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">OpenAI&#39;s first AI device could be a smart speaker</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/9fed010a-495e-4b9f-9ef2-9b9a93cddcb8/1771801268107.png?t=1771801283"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Lovart / The Rundown </p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>OpenAI-Jony Ive&#39;s first hardware product will <a class="link" href="https://www.theinformation.com/articles/inside-openai-team-developing-ai-devices?rc=a8sc5q&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=what-openai-and-jony-ive-are-building" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">reportedly be</a> a $200-$300 smart speaker with a built-in camera and facial recognition for purchases, according to The Information — backed by a 200+ team aiming to ship it by early 2027.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The team formed when OAI <a class="link" href="https://www.therundown.ai/p/openai-jony-ive-join-forces-in-6-5b-acquisition?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=what-openai-and-jony-ive-are-building" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">acquired</a> Ive&#39;s startup Io Products for $6.5B in May, bringing in Apple veterans to lead hardware, design, and supply chain.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The speaker&#39;s camera will allegedly observe surroundings and “nudge (users) toward actions”, with a Face ID-like facial recognition feature for purchases.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">AI-powered smart glasses are also planned, but won&#39;t hit production until at least 2028, with a smart lamp also created as a prototype. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OAI staffers have butted heads with LoveFrom over slow revisions and secrecy, with Ive&#39;s firm handling designs and the devices team working on the hardware.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>OAI has never shipped a physical product, but the mystique surrounding Jony Ive has made its hardware a hotly anticipated launch. With Apple <a class="link" href="https://www.rundown.ai/articles/anthropics-mid-tier-model-punches-up?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=what-openai-and-jony-ive-are-building" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">ramping up</a> AI device plans and Amazon already rolling with Alexa+, OAI&#39;s window to define the category is shrinking fast — making the speaker a very important first swing.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" class="image__link" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown</b> You wouldn’t expect a new employee to know everything without onboarding, would you? The same concept goes for AI agents—and metadata is the key.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>In this ebook, you’ll learn:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">How metadata management drives AI success</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Common pitfalls</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The ROI of proper metadata management</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://you.com/resources/mastering-metadata-management?utm_source=external-newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_campaign=32665437-Rundown_Q1&utm_term=rundown_primary_2.23&utm_content=rundown_primary_2.23" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Get the Ebook</a></span>.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">THE RUNDOWN ROUNDTABLE</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">💡<b><a class="link" href="https://www.therundown.ai/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=what-openai-and-jony-ive-are-building" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">The Rundown Roundtable: Our AI use cases</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/a421eb53-c47a-4745-9d6a-6465d5ed0d44/1771174224115.png?t=1771174241"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>The Rundown Roundtable is a weekly feature where we poll members of The Rundown staff about how we use AI in our work and daily lives.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Rowan, Founder & CEO: </b>As a fast-moving startup, many of our team&#39;s best ideas come from random Slack threads, but get lost and never fully hashed out. Instead of spending hours a day manually adding tasks to our databases, we used Notion&#39;s new Agents feature (rolling out soon for GA) and built an &quot;AI Project Manager&quot; that monitors Slack messages daily and logs tasks autonomously.<br><br><b>Shubham, Editor:</b> I used Gemini to analyze my blood work covering some 100 parameters. It instantly extracted and categorized all—from cholesterol to iron levels—into a clear, structured table, identified subtle deviations (such as slightly elevated eosinophils) and explained the clinical significance of each in plain language. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Finally, it translated these data points into a personalized wellness roadmap, suggesting natural lifestyle adjustments to optimize health markers.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Jennifer, Tech & Robotics Writer: </b>Over the past year, I’ve relied heavily on LLMs to support my French citizenship application— including drafting required letters and tracking paperwork. Although I’m already fluent, I used ChatGPT to prep for the required language exam to get familiar with the test format for 100% confidence.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;"><b>⚙️ </b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/how-to-self-host-n8n-5-minute-setup?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=what-openai-and-jony-ive-are-building" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><b>Self-host an n8n automation server in minutes</b></a></span></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/3d91aecf-74d2-4368-9260-b0db644b76db/CleanShot_2026-02-22_at_14.55.58_2x.png?t=1771794546"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you will learn to set up your own n8n automation server — helping you run thousands of automations per month on n8n with just a $5 virtual server. Best of all, you can set it up in under 10 minutes.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Go to <a class="link" href="https://railway.com/deploy/n8n?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=what-openai-and-jony-ive-are-building" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">railway.com/deploy/n8n</a>, sign in with GitHub, and click Deploy Now. You don’t need to configure any variables. Click Deploy on the next screen</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">After your automation server is deployed, click the n8n module, go to your custom link, and set up your email and password login</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Now, you can create a new automation by clicking Create workflow in your n8n dashboard — no need to set it up node-by-node</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Just ask Claude or ChatGPT to map out the automation you want as a JSON file. Then, in the new workflow, click the three dots, and import from file</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> You can invite users via email to your n8n server. This makes it great for client- or team-specific projects. You can even save API keys in the server for others to use. <br><br><i>For more tips on n8n + AI, check out our </i><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/courses/ai-automations-course?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=what-openai-and-jony-ive-are-building" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><i>AI Automations Course</i></a></span><i>.</i></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" href="https://taalas.com/the-path-to-ubiquitous-ai/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=what-openai-and-jony-ive-are-building" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">AI startup’s custom chip gives AI a 10x speed boost</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/5561ed6a-4728-4202-b69d-6f25bb90999a/taalas.jpg?t=1771795944"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Taalas</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>AI chip startup Taalas just <a class="link" href="https://taalas.com/the-path-to-ubiquitous-ai/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=what-openai-and-jony-ive-are-building" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">emerged</a> with HC1, a custom chip built to run a single AI model and nothing else — delivering responses roughly 100x faster than today&#39;s standard hardware and 10x the SOTA for extreme speed in outputs.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Taalas’ first chip permanently embeds Meta&#39;s Llama 3.1 8B model into the hardware rather than running it as software on general-purpose chips.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The result is near-instantaneous AI responses, with messages coming back in under 100 milliseconds at a fraction of the power and cost of other systems.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Llama 3.1 is small, older, and far from the frontier, but Taalas says it can retool chips for new models in just months — with a top-tier option planned by winter.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The startup pulled in $169M in new funding this round, bringing its total above $200M — with a mid-size reasoning model expected this spring.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>The model baked into the first chip is far from competitive, but the tech itself is the story. The speed needs to be seen to be comprehended (<a class="link" href="https://chatjimmy.ai/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=what-openai-and-jony-ive-are-building" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">demo here</a>) — and if the approach scales to frontier models, it could change what&#39;s possible in areas like physical AI or agentic workflows where every millisecond matters.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph"       <item>
  <title>Intelligence should be owned, not rented</title>
  <description>Inside Cisco’s strategy to scale agents securely and reshape enterprise workflows </description>
      <enclosure url="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/36d17aef-4f28-46ad-a4a4-c1f046f9a236/2026_Cisco_cover.png" length="1937245" type="image/png"/>

nofollow">Advertise</a></b></sup></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:5.0px 0.0px 5.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Good morning, {{ first_name | AI enthusiasts }}.</b> AI is often described as a “digital teammate,” but the reality is more complex. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Embedding AI systems into core workflows reshapes how teams operate — and raises some tough questions: What actually gets faster? What becomes riskier? And where must humans stay in control?</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">To unpack how this shift is playing out in practice, we sat down with DJ Sampath, SVP of AI Software and Platform at Cisco, on the sidelines of the <a class="link" href="https://www.ciscoaisummit.com/?utm_campaign=none&utm_medium=paid_social&utm_source=linkedin&utm_term=RunDown_Newsletter&utm_content=DJSampath_Takeover&utm_team=Social%C2%A0" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Cisco AI Summit</a> for a candid look at what it takes to build, secure, and scale with AI in the loop.</p><hr class="content_break"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>In today’s AI rundown:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The rise of a new agentic workforce</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Sampath’s structured, multi-model workflow</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Rethinking AI readiness from the ground up</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Today’s biggest AI security risk</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Why intelligence should be owned, not rented</p></li></ul></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:center;"><span style="color:#FFFFFF;"><b>LATEST DEVELOPMENTS</b></span></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AGENTIC SHIFT</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🤖 <a class="link" href="https://www.ciscoaisummit.com/?utm_campaign=none&utm_medium=paid_social&utm_source=linkedin&utm_term=RunDown_Newsletter&utm_content=DJSampath_Takeover&utm_team=Social%C2%A0" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b>The rise of a new agentic workforce</b></span></a></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://www.ciscoaisummit.com/?utm_campaign=none&utm_medium=paid_social&utm_source=linkedin&utm_term=RunDown_Newsletter&utm_content=DJSampath_Takeover&utm_team=Social%C2%A0" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/e764bd06-2dde-458c-a14b-3cd941b1c56c/2026_Cisco_cover.png?t=1771460420"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Cisco sees AI agents as a digital workforce that absorbs routine tasks (like outages), enabling teams to focus on the complex strategic work — and what comes next. The key takeaway for companies? Mastering human-agent collaboration.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Cheung: </b>Cisco has said AI will make the world feel like it has “80B people.” What does that mean inside a company? And how far can AI go in network ops?</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Sampath:</b> For the first time, we’re deploying digital teammates that can plan, reason, and execute with autonomy. Every leader will manage a constellation of agents working in parallel — investigating, analyzing, remediating — while humans move up the stack to creativity, judgment, and strategic direction.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Within 12 months, I expect AI to resolve roughly 80% of pattern-based, routine network incidents autonomously. The final 20%, which are multi-vendor, legacy-heavy, or edge-case complexities, will take longer. But just like self-driving, progress will compound.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Sampath added:</b> Over the next five years, the companies that learn to design for human–agent collaboration, with trust, governance, and intent at the core, will define the next era of operational performance.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Humans won’t be replaced by AI, but they will be pushed up the stack. As agents absorb the predictable and procedural, the premium will shift to judgment, creativity, and strategic thinking. The winning edge for businesses will come from pairing that human depth with agents’ speed and scale.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">DJ’S WORKFLOW</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🔥 <a class="link" href="https://www.ciscoaisummit.com/?utm_campaign=none&utm_medium=paid_social&utm_source=linkedin&utm_term=RunDown_Newsletter&utm_content=DJSampath_Takeover&utm_team=Social%C2%A0" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b>Sampath’s structured, multi-model workflow</b></span></a></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://www.ciscoaisummit.com/?utm_campaign=none&utm_medium=paid_social&utm_source=linkedin&utm_term=RunDown_Newsletter&utm_content=DJSampath_Takeover&utm_team=Social%C2%A0" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/9891b691-3bef-4153-8328-ca22991f056d/01_Sampath_s_structured__multi-model_workflow.png?t=1771460444"/></a><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image: Kiki Wu / The Rundown</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Sampath practices what he preaches — using AI to rethink how work gets done daily. From multi-model ideation to coding agents that automate daily briefs, here’s how Cisco’s head of AI actually uses the technology.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Cheung:</b> What kind of workflows are you automating with AI? Can you give a few examples?</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Sampath</b>: At work, I’ve been experimenting with a simple but structured way of using multiple AI tools. First, I separate idea generation from evaluation by drafting a memo, strategy, or customer narrative in one model, then bringing it into a second model to critique and improve it. This helps me think more clearly and produce stronger work.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Next, I use Cursor to store context in markdown files and folders that AI can reference. Over time, this builds a knowledge base, like a long-term thought partner that understands my frameworks and past work.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Sampath added:</b> I also connect AI to my calendar and meeting notes to review context before customer, partner, or analyst conversations. Plus, I’ve started using coding agents to automate work like daily briefs, product reviews, and document analysis. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Sampath’s approach shows that the future of work will be defined by how teams stitch together agents, models, and systems into structured but adaptable workflows. The Cursor-as-knowledge-base idea is especially actionable, turning one-off AI interactions into a compounding system that gets smarter over time.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI READINESS</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🦄 <a class="link" href="https://www.cisco.com/c/dam/m/en_us/solutions/ai/readiness-index/2025-m10/documents/cisco-ai-readiness-index-2025-realizing-the-value-of-ai.pdf?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=intelligence-should-be-owned-not-rented" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><b><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Rethinking AI readiness from the ground up</span></b></a></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://www.cisco.com/c/dam/m/en_us/solutions/ai/readiness-index/2025-m10/documents/cisco-ai-readiness-index-2025-realizing-the-value-of-ai.pdf?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=intelligence-should-be-owned-not-rented" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/bfff84b5-d2d5-47af-bbc9-c18021485c31/02_Rethinking-AI-readiness-from-the-ground_up.png?t=1771460505"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Most enterprises are held back from AI adoption not by a lack of ambition, but by infrastructure debt and siloed data. Sampath says the real unlock requires pairing modern infrastructure with leadership clarity — and embedding intelligence directly into products.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Cheung: </b><a class="link" href="https://www.cisco.com/c/dam/m/en_us/solutions/ai/readiness-index/2025-m10/documents/cisco-ai-readiness-index-2025-realizing-the-value-of-ai.pdf?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=intelligence-should-be-owned-not-rented" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Cisco&#39;s AI Readiness Index</a> shows only 28% of organizations believe they’re ready for AI workloads. What’s holding back the rest, and what does it take to be a true AI company today?</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Sampath:</b> What’s holding back the other 72% isn’t just missing GPUs. It’s AI infrastructure debt: legacy networks, fragmented data, siloed tooling. Systems built for yesterday’s applications can’t support the throughput, real-time processing, and autonomy that modern AI demands.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Another key component is the need to pair modern infrastructure with leadership clarity — governance, strategy, and alignment to business outcomes. The leaders have to solve for both, defining tech and how work will happen with AI.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Sampath added:</b> The sustainable advantage will come when intelligence is embedded into the product itself. When the model is trained on your contextual enterprise data, it improves continuously and directly drives outcomes. So, the product becomes the model, and the model becomes the product.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Being “AI-ready” means rethinking the whole stack, from infra to security to the application layer. Companies that make AI core to their product (not just a feature) can unlock feedback loops backed by proprietary data, where outcomes improve continuously and enable them to move faster.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;"> AI SECURITY</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🧠 <a class="link" href="https://blogs.cisco.com/ai/cisco-state-of-ai-security-2026-report?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=intelligence-should-be-owned-not-rented" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b>Today’s biggest AI security risk</b></span></a></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://blogs.cisco.com/ai/cisco-state-of-ai-security-2026-report?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=intelligence-should-be-owned-not-rented" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/86512eae-2feb-45c5-9a2f-19b02ac8f3a4/3_Today_s_biggest_AI_security_risk.png?t=1771430359"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> Sampath says that the most urgent AI security threat is the risk of agent compromise. As these systems take on more tasks, they become powerful attack surfaces — with the risk only growing with time.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Cheung: </b>What&#39;s the most concrete, real AI security threat right now?</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Sampath: </b>The most immediate <a class="link" href="https://blogs.cisco.com/ai/cisco-state-of-ai-security-2026-report?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=intelligence-should-be-owned-not-rented" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">AI security risk</a> is the compromise and misuse of autonomous agents. As enterprises deploy agentic systems that access data, invoke tools, and make decisions independently, those agents become a new attack surface. They can be hijacked, impersonated, or manipulated to exfiltrate data or execute unauthorized commands at machine speed.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">We’re already seeing attackers probe these gaps. That’s why we consider AI security from two perspectives: protecting the enterprise from agents and protecting agents from the world — with zero-trust identity, control over agent protocols and tool registries, and continuous behavioral monitoring.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Cheung: </b>If an enterprise is moving from AI pilots to production, what’s the first system they need to harden? And where should a human always stay in the loop?</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Sampath: </b>The first thing to harden is the agent infrastructure. The real risk sits in the connective tissue: the protocols that link agents to tools, data, and each other. Standards like Model Context Protocol and agent-to-agent have become the backbone of autonomous workflows, but they scaled faster than the security around them.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">As teams roll out agentic AI, anything that affects trust, access, or control over critical systems — granting privileges, changing production environments, authorizing sensitive data access, initiating irreversible actions — should never run fully autonomous. When consequences are real, accountability has to be human.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The right model isn’t human-out-of-the-loop. It’s AI-in-the-loop. Let agents handle the routine and low-risk at speed, and keep humans as the authority where impact is high.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters:</b> The shift from models that answer to agents that act introduces a new class of risk — systemic, fast-moving, and hard to contain. To secure operations in this future, organizations will have to bake their agentic deployments with identity, guardrails, and constant oversight, treating them like real entities.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">THE AI COMPANY THESIS</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">⚡️ <a class="link" href="https://www.ciscoaisummit.com/?utm_campaign=none&utm_medium=paid_social&utm_source=linkedin&utm_term=RunDown_Newsletter&utm_content=DJSampath_Takeover&utm_team=Social%C2%A0" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b>Why intelligence should be owned, not rented</b></span></a></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://www.ciscoaisummit.com/?utm_campaign=none&utm_medium=paid_social&utm_source=linkedin&utm_term=RunDown_Newsletter&utm_content=DJSampath_Takeover&utm_team=Social%C2%A0" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/084829ee-9f57-4176-b03f-e83d6417f0a1/04__Why_intelligence_should_be_owned__not_rented.png?t=1771430379"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Many companies are racing to bolt AI onto existing products, but Sampath argues the real moat comes from embedding intelligence into the product itself — and makes a bold case that the future of AI shouldn’t be controlled by a handful of centralized providers.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Cheung: </b>You’ve said “companies that are a thin shim on top of a model — their days are numbered.” What does that actually mean?</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Sampath:</b> We mean this: adding a generative API to an existing product isn’t a strategy — it’s a feature.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Sustainable advantage comes when intelligence is embedded into the product itself. When the model is trained on your contextual enterprise data, it improves continuously and directly drives outcomes. That closed loop — fueled by proprietary machine data — is the moat.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Cheung: </b>If you weren’t at Cisco, what AI problem would you want to work on?</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Sampath:</b> The problem I care most about is ownership of intelligence. I don’t believe the future belongs to a handful of centralized models controlled by a few providers. I believe intelligence should be owned by enterprises — and ultimately, by individuals.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">That means building a full stack that allows organizations to develop, fine-tune, deploy, and govern models on their own terms.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>“Intelligence should be owned, not rented” is an interesting thesis when most enterprises currently leverage centralized AI providers. It raises a question every company should be asking: are you building AI capabilities that compound over time, or renting them from someone who could eventually change the terms?</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:center;"><span style="color:#FFFFFF;"><b>GO DEEPER</b></span></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI SUMMIT</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">📺 <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">W</a></b></span><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://www.ciscoaisummit.com/?utm_campaign=none&utm_medium=paid_social&utm_source=linkedin&utm_term=RunDown_Newsletter&utm_content=DJSampath_Takeover&utm_team=Social%C2%A0" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">atch the Cisco AI Summit on-demand</a></b></span></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://www.ciscoaisummit.com/?utm_campaign=none&utm_medium=paid_social&utm_source=linkedin&utm_term=RunDown_Newsletter&utm_content=DJSampath_Takeover&utm_team=Social%C2%A0" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/7bad54e0-4157-4162-bd67-b656b146998a/CAIS_1200_social.jpg?t=1771460554"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Watch all of the sessions from the Cisco AI Summit on-demand, featuring discussions including:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Google</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Google just <a class="link" href="https://blog.google/innovation-and-ai/models-and-research/gemini-models/gemini-3-1-pro/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-handshake-refusal-heard-around-the-ai-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">released</a> Gemini 3.1 Pro, bringing a massive reasoning upgrade, benchmark-topping performance, and overall SOTA capabilities while keeping API pricing identical to its predecessor.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">3.1 Pro scored 77.1% on the identical to 3 Pro with the same 1M token context window, coming in cheaper than frontier model options from Anthropic and OpenAI. </p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it We expect a counter answer from OpenAI sooner rather than later. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">✏️ <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/write-viral-youtube-scripts-with-this-free-tool?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-handshake-refusal-heard-around-the-ai-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Write viral YouTube scripts with NotebookLM</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/09c57268-6fe9-4f98-b1fd-70048c8b775a/nbtutorial.jpg?t=1771541993"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you will learn to use NotebookLM to “watch” YouTube videos for you, then turn them into ideas and scripts for your own videos.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Find a long-form YouTube video that you like the structure of. Go to <a class="link" href="https://notebooklm.google.com?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-handshake-refusal-heard-around-the-ai-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">NotebookLM</a> &gt; Create new &gt; Add sources &gt; Websites and paste the link in</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Once NotebookLM analyzes it, make sure it’s selected, and prompt: “Reverse engineer the structure of this video. Give me a video outline and 4 video concepts with the same structure for my brand, [brand]”</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Select the video concept you like best and instruct GoogleLM to generate a script for that idea. Click Save to note &gt; click the three dots &gt; Export to Docs</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Now you have a script in Google Docs that’s ready to record</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> You can save your best scripts as sources to give NotebookLM a better idea of what you like.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px the guide today</a></span> and learn how to build better AI agent.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="text-align:left;">AI AT WORK</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">👀 <b><a class="link" href="https://www.ft.com/content/ac672f97-a603-4c56-afa3-4a5273d45674?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-handshake-refusal-heard-around-the-ai-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Corporate giant Accenture ties AI usage to promotions</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/c994843e-c013-4644-a850-bbd22fa5e876/1771543846698.png?t=1771543854"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Lovart / The Rundown</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Consulting giant Accenture is now reportedly <a class="link" href="https://www.ft.com/content/ac672f97-a603-4c56-afa3-4a5273d45674?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=the-handshake-refusal-heard-around-the-ai-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">monitoring</a> weekly AI tool usage for senior employees and tying adoption directly to leadership promotions, in an attempt to bring veteran staff on board with the tech’s rising use in the workplace. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Three consulting execs told FT that getting senior partners to adopt AI is far harder than with junior staff, a firmwide seniority problem across the industry.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Associate directors aiming for promotions will now have AI tool logins tracked weekly, with usage flagged as a &quot;visible input&quot; to leadership reviews.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Accenture says 550K+ of its 780K staff have gone through AI training, though employees called the AI tools used in-house “broken slop generators”. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">CEO Julie Sweet made headlines last year when she said on an earnings call that the firm would “exit” staff who don’t reskill for AI’s rise. </p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>There is some irony in the senior employees being unwilling to adapt to the AI boom at the same time the tech is eating entry-level positions. But the wave of job transformation is here, and not learning AI will be a far more rapid equivalent of resisting the internet when it comes to competing and succeeding at work. </p></div><p href="https://blog.google/innovation-and-ai/products/gemini-app/lyria-3/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-brings-ai-music-to-the-masses" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Google brings AI music creation into Gemini</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/1eb1f9dd-5971-484d-8be0-05101913ffde/lyria3.jpg?t=1771441925"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Google</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Google just <a class="link" href="https://blog.google/innovation-and-ai/products/gemini-app/lyria-3/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-brings-ai-music-to-the-masses" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">rolled out</a> Lyria 3 in Gemini, the company’s new AI music generation model — letting users turn a text prompt or photo into customized, 30-second tracks with auto-generated lyrics and cover art.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The model handles everything from genre and tempo to vocal style and lyrics on its own, with users able to feed text, photos, or videos as a starting point.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">DeepMind has been working on Lyria since 2023, but this marks the first time the tech is reaching the main consumer audience through the Gemini app.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Every track gets tagged with Google&#39;s SynthID watermark, with Gemini also allowing users to upload any audio file to check whether it was created with AI.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">YouTube creators are also getting access to Lyria 3 through Dream Track for Shorts, enabling easily customized audio tracks to accompany video posts. </p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>AI music platforms like Suno and Udio have quietly gotten scary good, producing full tracks that can fool most listeners — but are still far from ‘mainstream’. Embedding Lyria inside Gemini is a different beast, putting AI music creation a prompt away for millions of users who&#39;ve likely never even heard of a dedicated music model. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">TOGETHER WITH VISA</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">👋 <b><a class="link" href="https://link.therundown.ai/lcr46g?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-brings-ai-music-to-the-masses" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Meet Visa Intelligent Commerce</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://link.therundown.ai/lcr46g?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-brings-ai-music-to-the-masses" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/3a22b45c-1356-414f-b322-9006070e3f8e/visa-trd.jpg?t=1771435374"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>The groundbreaking framework that enables AI agents to find and buy.
