style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/ef5922df-ea67-41e5-b7c4-c5e25bbc8f88/1771446515167.jpg?t=1771446529"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Lovart / The Rundown</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>OpenAI <a class="link" href="https://www.vanityfair.com/news/story/openai-hires-charles-porch-instagram?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-brings-ai-music-to-the-masses" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">hired</a> Meta&#39;s longtime celebrity partnerships chief Charles Porch as its VP of global creative partnerships, according to Vanity Fair — a new role aimed at bridging the gap between the AI giant and a distrusting entertainment industry.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Porch spent 15+ years as the go-to exec for getting A-listers onto IG, handling viral moments like Beyonce’s 2013 album drop and onboarding the Pope. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The hire follows OAI&#39;s $1B Disney deal in December, which opened its Sora video platform up to animated characters from Marvel, Pixar, and Star Wars.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Porch says his first move will be a &quot;listening tour&quot; across creative communities this spring, reporting to OAI&#39;s applications CEO Fidji Simo.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>While we’ve seen celebs move into platforms like ElevenLabs, the broader Hollywood sentiment towards AI has been frigid at best. Porch&#39;s deep rolodex and reputation as a translator between tech and talent make him the kind of person who can help gain trust in rooms with names that could shift sentiment for the industry. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">📸 <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/turn-product-photos-into-scroll-stopping-video-content?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-brings-ai-music-to-the-masses" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Turn product photos into scroll-stopping videos</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/fbc8f67f-3769-47be-8fb9-bf8958441512/CleanShot_2026-02-18_at_16.34.08_2x.png?t=1771456827"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you&#39;ll learn how to turn a product photo into a cinematic clip ready for social media using Runway&#39;s video generation tool. This method excels at creating consistent clips that are ready for ad campaigns and product announcements.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Grab a product photo first — Runway will use it for the start frame. Don’t have a product? Use a software mockup or ask Gemini to generate one for the brand</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Drop the photo into any AI, prompting: &quot;Write me a brief video prompt to use in Runway to generate a social media video based on this product photo. Add animations and/or camera movement if applicable&quot;</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Next, go to <a class="link" href="https://Runwayml.com?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-brings-ai-music-to-the-masses" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Runway</a> &gt; Tool &gt; Video and add your starting frame and the AI-generated prompt</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Rinse and repeat for the rest of your product photos. Try different combinations of text overlay and music when you post them to socials</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> This is also a great way to enhance your existing ad sets — try adding them to your in Google or Meta campaigns.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PRESENTED BY VANTA</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🔒 <b><a class="link" href="https://www.vanta.com/downloads/on-demand-demo?utm_campaign=on-demand-demo&utm_source=the-rundown-ai&utm_medium=newsletter" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Compliance just got 82% faster</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://www.vanta.com/downloads/on-demand-demo?utm_campaign=on-demand-demo&utm_source=the-rundown-ai&utm_medium=newsletter" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/8d233d41-0db1-4179-943c-e76ea15bd53e/image1__19_.jpg?t=1771436413"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> Risk and regulations are ramping up, and customers now expect proof of security just to do business. Vanta brings compliance, risk, and customer trust together on one AI-powered platform — so you stay secure and keep deals moving.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>With Vanta, you can:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Automate up to 90% of the work for SOC 2, ISO 27001, HIPAA, and more</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Streamline security reviews with AI-powered questionnaires</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Spend 82% less time on audits, like companies including Ramp and Writer</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://www.vanta.com/downloads/on-demand-demo?utm_campaign=on-demand-demo&utm_source=the-rundown-ai&utm_medium=newsletter" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Watch the on-demand demo</a></span> to see how Vanta works.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI RESEARCH</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🗣️ <b><a class="link" href="https://www.tavus.io/post/phoenix-4-real-time-human-rendering-with-emotional-intelligence?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-brings-ai-music-to-the-masses" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Tavus’ new AI avatars actually read the room</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/effd3c09-690b-4ed8-afcc-96fdf1f34df8/phoenix4.jpg?t=1771458161"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Tavus</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> Tavus just <a class="link" href="https://www.tavus.io/post/phoenix-4-real-time-human-rendering-with-emotional-intelligence?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-brings-ai-music-to-the-masses" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">introduced</a> Phoenix-4, a real-time human rendering model that can generate AI avatars that have full facial expressions, shift between emotions mid-conversation, and actively listen with contextual reactions. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Phoenix-4 generates every pixel of the face and head from scratch each frame, trained on thousands of hours of real human conversation.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The model handles 10+ emotional states and transitions between them in real time, avoiding awkward mismatched reactions or expressions during convos.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Tavus is pitching the tech for healthcare, education, and sales use cases where feeling &quot;heard&quot; by the person on screen can directly impact outcomes. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Phoenix-4 also runs at HD quality and at 40 FPS for live video call smoothness, making interactions feel more real than older model generations.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>AI text interactions are becoming more human than ever, and video avatars are now catching up to the pace — leaving the hollow ‘uncanny valley’ of robotic emotion for a conversation partner that feels like it’s actually listening. The positive applications are endless… But so are the coming opportunities for deception. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:center;"><span style="color:#FFFFFF;"><b>QUICK HITS</b></span></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="text-align:left;"><b>Meta and Nvidia </b><a class="link" href="https://nvidianews.nvidia.com/news/meta-builds-ai-infrastructure-with-nvidia?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-s-mid-tier-model-punches-up" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">announced</a> a new multiyear AI chip deal spanning millions of GPUs and CPUs to help power the tech giant’s AI infrastructure buildout.</p><p nofollow">open-sourced</a> Tiny Aya, a 3.35B parameter multilingual model that handles 70+ languages with strong gains for typically underrepresented dialects.</p><p class="paragraph" website design.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px risk” in response to the company’s limits on how the military uses its AI.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The feud, which only appears to be escalating, highlights a deeper tension now shaping the AI era: who controls how frontier models are deployed in military operations — the labs that build them, or the governments that use them?</p><hr class="content_break"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>In today’s AI rundown:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Anthropic-Pentagon feud escalates over AI use</p></li><li><p style="text-align:left;">ANTHROPIC</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">‼️ <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://www.axios.com/2026/02/15/claude-pentagon-anthropic-contract-maduro?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery&_bhlid=147fc2fb115d35bbc6b2211e9bcebfff031af136" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Anthropic-Pentagon feud escalates over AI use</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/22c18828-df37-4ca4-ad0d-b2fe286f064c/Refined_Color_Tone.png?t=1771321961"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Nano Banana / The Rundown</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>The Pentagon is reportedly “close” to <a class="link" href="https://www.axios.com/2026/02/15/claude-pentagon-anthropic-contract-maduro?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery&_bhlid=147fc2fb115d35bbc6b2211e9bcebfff031af136" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">cutting ties</a> with Anthropic and designating the company a “supply chain risk” — a badge usually reserved for foreign adversaries — over its restrictions on how Claude is used by the military.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The designation of “supply chain risk,” if given, would force all U.S. defense contractors to cut ties with Anthropic — hitting the AI’s major business severely.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Defense officials are demanding the right to use AI for “all lawful purposes,” while Anthropic is holding firm against granting broad permissions.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The company is open to loosening restrictions but wants to ensure its AI is not used for spying on Americans or building autonomous weapons, Axios reports.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Claude is currently the only AI on the Pentagon’s classified systems, and was also <a class="link" href="https://www.wsj.com/politics/national-security/pentagon-used-anthropics-claude-in-maduro-venezuela-raid-583aff17?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-pentagon-ai-feud-escalates" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">reportedly</a> used via Palantir to capture Nicolás Maduro in January.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Experts have long warned about the unchecked use of AI in warfare, and this standoff marks a notable moment showing the growing friction between companies’ responsible-use guardrails and the military’s operational demands. Only time will tell which side shapes the rules of AI in national security.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">TOGETHER WITH YOU.COM</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🧠 <a class="link" href="https://you.com/resources/2026-ai-predictions?utm_campaign=32665437-Rundown_Q1&utm_source=external-newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_term=rundown_primary_2.3&utm_content=rundown_primary_2.3" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><b><span style="text-decoration:underline;">You.com founders predict an AI winter is coming</span></b></a></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://you.com/resources/2026-ai-predictions?utm_campaign=32665437-Rundown_Q1&utm_source=external-newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_term=rundown_primary_2.3&utm_content=rundown_primary_2.3" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/7181483e-6457-40c9-a29d-1d7ea79dcdbd/image2.png?t=1771295951"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown</b>: <a class="link" href="https://you.com/resources/2026-ai-predictions?utm_campaign=32665437-Rundown_Q1&utm_source=external-newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_term=rundown_primary_2.3&utm_content=rundown_primary_2.3" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">You.com</a>’s Co-founders Richard Socher and Bryan McCann are among the most-cited AI researchers in the world. They just released 35 predictions for 2026.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Three that stand out:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The LLM revolution has been “mined out” as capital floods back to research</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">“Reward engineering” becomes a job; prompts can’t handle what’s coming next</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Traditional coding will be gone by December — AI writes code and humans manage it</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><a class="link" href="https://you.com/resources/2026-ai-predictions?utm_campaign=32665437-Rundown_Q1&utm_source=external-newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_term=rundown_primary_2.3&utm_content=rundown_primary_2.3" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Read all 35 predictions</span></a>.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">OPENAI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🔒️ <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/introducing-lockdown-mode-and-elevated-risk-labels-in-chatgpt/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-pentagon-ai-feud-escalates" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">OpenAI adds ‘Lockdown Mode’ to ChatGPT</a></b></span></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/1673aac8-21e2-4829-819f-bcd92d4c1802/Cleaned_Image__1_.png?t=1771317882"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Reve / The Rundown</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>OpenAI just <a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/introducing-lockdown-mode-and-elevated-risk-labels-in-chatgpt/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-pentagon-ai-feud-escalates" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">introduced</a> a “Lockdown Mode” in ChatGPT, alongside new Elevated Risk labels, as part of an effort to protect “highly security-conscious users” from threats like prompt injection (where AI is tricked into leaking data).</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The Lockdown Mode is an optional setting that deterministically disables certain ChatGPT tools and capabilities that an attacker could exploit.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Specific protections in the mode include limiting web browsing to cached content — ensuring no live network requests leave OpenAI’s environment.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">ChatGPT workspace admins can enable the mode, with the ability to whitelist specific apps/actions that remain accessible even when the lockdown is active.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The company is also adding new “Elevated Risk” labels that appear across ChatGPT, Atlas, and Codex to flag features that may introduce any level of risk.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>As AI models go from simple chatbots to full-fledged agents capable of browsing the web, connecting to apps, and executing complex tasks, the security stakes are higher than ever. This update acknowledges that change and the fact that deterministic “hard blocks” may be the only way to address some AI risks.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">📲 <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/how-to-turn-one-youtube-thumbnail-into-5-different-social-posts?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-pentagon-ai-feud-escalates" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Turn a YouTube thumbnail into 5 social posts</a></b></span></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/01f32f71-3eb4-4930-92f5-c1625d290682/CleanShot_2026-02-16_at_16.12.40_2x.png?t=1771296480"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you will build a YouTube thumbnail from scratch in Canva, then use the AI resize feature to instantly duplicate it into every social media format, with AI handling the layout for each size.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">In <a class="link" href="http://canva.com?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-pentagon-ai-feud-escalates" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Canva</a> (you will need a Pro account), click the “Create” button and search for “thumbnail.” Click the YouTube thumbnail project type</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">In the sidebar, pick a template that you like. Update the text to match your video title and change the colors if you want</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">If there’s a cutout person in it, you can take a selfie, drag it into Canva, then click the AI remove background button. Now, replace the placeholder cutout</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Finally, click the “Resize” in the top left and select all social placements you want. Canva AI will create thumbnail layouts in the correct dimensions for each</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> You can also generate thumbnails using Nano Banana Pro, then recreate them in Canva.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PRESENTED BY SPEECHMATICS</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🗣️ <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://www.speechmatics.com/best-ears-in-ai?utm_source=rundown-ai&utm_medium=paid-media&utm_campaign=voice-agents&utm_content=newsletter" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Voice Agents need speed you trust</a></b></span></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://www.speechmatics.com/best-ears-in-ai?utm_source=rundown-ai&utm_medium=paid-media&utm_campaign=voice-agents&utm_content=newsletter" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/d002cbf8-17f8-4dd7-a904-d2e3acfa24e5/image4.png?t=1771296155"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> Speechmatics’ Voice Agent API delivers partials in &lt;250ms and finals around 250-300ms. Built real-time first, not batch models forced into streaming. That’s why you get unmatched accuracy at conversational latency.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>What you get:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">55+ languages, accent-agnostic performance</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Native LiveKit, Pipecat, Vapi support</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Deploy cloud, on-prem, hybrid, on-device</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://www.speechmatics.com/best-ears-in-ai?utm_source=rundown-ai&utm_medium=paid-media&utm_campaign=voice-agents&utm_content=newsletter" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Start building</a></span> with <b>$200 free credits</b>.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">ALIBABA</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🧠 <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://qwen.ai/blog?id=qwen3.5&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-pentagon-ai-feud-escalates" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Alibaba nears frontier with open-weight Qwen-3.5</a></b></span></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/c8516b24-fc3f-4f3d-adc8-5d85097d3717/Untitled_design.png?t=1771318641"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Qwen </p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Alibaba’s Qwen <a class="link" href="https://qwen.ai/blog?id=qwen3.5&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-pentagon-ai-feud-escalates" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">released</a> Qwen3.5-397B-A17B, an open-weight vision language model featuring a “hybrid architecture” that delivers massive inference gains while rivaling proprietary giants like OpenAI’s GPT-5.2 and Google’s Gemini 3 Pro.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Qwen-3.5 uses a sparse MoE design, activating only 17B parameters out of 397B for each query, balancing high-level capabilities with low latency.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The model is close to frontier players across the board, and even surpasses them in domains like agentic search, doc recognition, and instruction following.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Alibaba claims it is 60% cheaper to use and at least 8x better at processing large workloads than its immediate predecessor, Qwen3-Max.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The release is aimed at handling continuous, multimodal reasoning required by agents, although it doesn’t seem <a class="link" href="https://x.com/andonlabs/status/2023450768406364238?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-pentagon-ai-feud-escalates" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">very good</a> at running a vending machine yet.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Chinese labs are on a roll, and with Qwen3.5 combining near frontier performance, 60% lower costs, and open weights, the race is clearly shifting toward efficiency and scalability. If the momentum continues, the AI balance may hinge less on raw size and more on who can deliver powerful models at the lowest rate.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:center;"><span style="color:#FFFFFF;"><b>QUICK HITS</b></span></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h3 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🛠️ <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://www.rundown.ai/tools?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-pentagon-ai-feud-escalates" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Trending AI Tools</a></b></span></h3><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">👨‍💻 <span style="color:inherit;"><a class="link" href="https://link.therundown.ai/CTAYUK?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=anthropic-pentagon-ai-feud-escalates" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><b>HeyGen</b></a></span> - Turn ideas into videos in minutes, with no filming required. 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">OPENAI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🔬 <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/new-result-theoretical-physics/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">GPT-5.2 makes theoretical physics discovery</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/82540076-c25c-4cfd-9d48-c3c8b55705e6/Robotic_Einstein_Clean_Tongue.png?t=1771182083"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Lovart / The Rundown</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>OpenAI just <a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/new-result-theoretical-physics/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">published</a> a new research preprint where GPT-5.2 independently discovered a mathematical formula and formally proved it was correct, marking what the company calls AI&#39;s first original contribution to theoretical physics.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The <a class="link" href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.12176?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">paper</a> tackles a problem in particle physics that was assumed solved, with 5.2 finding the existing answer was wrong and proposing a correct one.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">A specialized research version of 5.2 autonomously wrote the math proof in 12 hours, verified by physicists from Harvard, Cambridge, and Princeton.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OAI&#39;s Kevin Weil is credited as a co-author, with Harvard physicist Andrew Strominger saying the AI &quot;chose a path no human would have tried.&quot;</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>There will still be debate from skeptics over whether AI is truly capable of ‘new’ ideas, but the results are getting harder to argue with. AI being pointed at and challenging long-held beliefs in humanity’s most important scientific fields is starting to feel less like sci-fi and more like the very near future. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px class="heading" style="text-align:left;">THE RUNDOWN ROUNDTABLE</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">💡<a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">The Rundown Roundtable: Our AI use cases</span></a></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/a421eb53-c47a-4745-9d6a-6465d5ed0d44/1771174224115.png?t=1771174240"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image Source: Lovart / The Rundown</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>The Rundown Roundtable is a weekly feature where we poll members of The Rundown staff about how we use AI in our work and daily lives.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Rishi, Growth: </b>I connected Claude Code to Apify&#39;s API to scrape high-performing content from IG/TikTok for ad creative inspiration, and to ElevenLabs&#39; API to automatically transcribe videos — so I can analyze not just visuals, but the exact hooks, pacing, and language top creators are using. From there, I developed a scriptwriting system that takes rough thoughts on a hook and angle and turns them into ad scripts, drawing inspiration from winners and applying proven copywriting principles.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">After generating, it also grades itself against a 12-point rubric. If it doesn&#39;t score at least 90%, it rewrites until it does. I then feed it back in and say, &quot;This is the final version.&quot; It analyzes the changes I made and updates its understanding of my style.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Nate, University Educator: </b>I continue to find that Claude Artifacts (with its front-end design) is delightfully useful — and use it several times a day to learn something new, or catch up on a news story, and turn anything into a custom webpage right inside chat.<br><br>Attach surveys, <a class="link" href="https://claude.ai/public/artifacts/72b06e04-5703-4541-bc36-d4b5170eda0e?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">a long article</a>, a spreadsheet, etc., and tell Claude to turn it into an interactive page displaying key insights. The design is impressive, and it takes just minutes. Next time, try this to quickly share findings with your team.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">📞<a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/launch-an-ai-powered-outbound-calling-agent-in-15-minutes?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" style="color: inherit"> </a><b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/launch-an-ai-powered-outbound-calling-agent-in-15-minutes?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Launch an outbound calling agent in 15 minutes</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/892fe4ab-fd60-4cf8-b937-cfa8abafd8c2/CleanShot_2026-02-15_at_16.46.54_2x.png?t=1771192135"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you will build an AI agent that makes real sales calls on your behalf. You’ll learn to create the agent, get a $1 phone number, and upload a list of contacts for it to call — with the whole setup taking about 15 minutes.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Create a new AI agent in <a class="link" href="https://elevenlabs.io?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Eleven Labs</a>. Choose a voice and add system instructions. Include details about your business, offer, and the goal of the call</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Sign up on <a class="link" href="http://twilio.com?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Twilio</a> (free + $15 in credits) and buy a phone number for $1.20. Copy the number, Account SID, and Auth Token from the dashboard</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Connect Twilio to Eleven Labs. Go to Phone Numbers in ElevenLabs, click Create New, and paste in your number, SID, and Auth Token</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Click Outbound in ElevenLabs, create a “batch” with Telephony as the channel, and download a CSV template. Add in leads’ numbers, then upload the CSV back. You can now start calling with the agent, test it, or schedule calls for later.</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> Toggle on “Transfer to Number” in your agent&#39;s Tools to have it patch hot leads through to your phone.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PRESENTED BY CONCIERGE</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">👋 <b><a class="link" href="https://link.therundown.ai/I1nXe8?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Your brand&#39;s AI answer engine</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://link.therundown.ai/I1nXe8?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/24e82a63-b330-48b7-9185-e501815b0906/image1__49_.png?t=1771173579"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> Today’s buyers use AI every day to answer their questions, and have no patience for a scavenger hunt on your website. nofollow">shared</a> new test results showing its 2-hour, AI-first academic model has students scoring in the 99th percentile across virtually every grade and subject.</p><p class="paragraph" href="https://x.com/simile_ai/status/2022011618176237657?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">raised</a> $100M to build AI simulations of human behavior, with agents modeled on real people to help companies predict customer decisions.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:center;"><span style="color:#FFFFFF;"><b>COMMUNITY</b></span></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h3 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🤝 <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSfH4UPzu72HTpdb08Qlm-0dLwKJIjdcAwCcAvVywcHD6mwKig/viewform?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-s-new-physics-discovery" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Community AI workflows</a></b></span></h3><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Every newsletter, we showcase how a reader is using AI to work smarter, save time, or make life easier.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Today’s workflow comes from reader <b>Peter S.</b> in Hollis, NH:</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">&quot;We recently had a water pipe break in our basement, causing damage to the items we store there. The insurance company required us to itemize, take pictures, and provide an estimated replacement cost for each damaged item.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Instead of searching websites, I uploaded the photos in Copilot with descriptions to obtain a good estimate and several links to where we can buy the items. What would have been days to complete the inventory list turned into a couple of hours.&quot;</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">How do you use AI? style="text-align:left;">GOOGLE</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;"><b>⚡</b><a class="link" href="https://blog.google/innovation-and-ai/models-and-research/gemini-models/gemini-3-deep-think/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-s-upgrade-breaks-reasoning-barriers" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b>Google&#39;s Deep Think crushes reasoning benchmarks</b></span></a></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/f7ca6186-bd58-410b-8653-a3027a8f7ae9/deepthink.jpg?t=1770928318"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Google</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Google just <a class="link" href="https://blog.google/innovation-and-ai/models-and-research/gemini-models/gemini-3-deep-think/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-s-upgrade-breaks-reasoning-barriers" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">released</a> a major update to its Gemini 3 Deep Think reasoning mode, posting dominant scores across math, coding, and science — while also introducing its Olympiad-level math research agent driven by the new upgrade.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Deep Think hit 84.6% on ARC-AGI-2, obliterating Opus 4.6 (68.8%) and GPT-5.2 (52.9%), and set a new high of 48.4% on Humanity&#39;s Last Exam.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">It also reached gold-medal marks on the 2025 Physics & Chemistry Olympiads and scored a 3,455 Elo on Codeforces, nearly 1,000 points above Opus 4.6.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Google also <a class="link" href="https://deepmind.google/blog/accelerating-mathematical-and-scientific-discovery-with-gemini-deep-think/?utm_source=x&utm_medium=social&utm_campaign=&utm_content=" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">unveiled</a> Aletheia, a math agent that autonomously solves open problems, verifies proofs, and hits new highs across domain benchmarks.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The Deep Think upgrade is live for Google AI Ultra subscribers in the Gemini app, with API access open to researchers via an early access program.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>After Google dominated benchmarks and headlines to close 2025, the focus has been more on Anthropic and OpenAI in 2026 — but don’t forget about the tech giant as arguably the biggest powerhouse in the AI race. Deep Think’s scores are wild, and the frontier for math and science is quickly moving into uncharted territory.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">TOGETHER WITH VOXEL51</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">💸 <b><a class="link" href="https://link.voxel51.com/the-rundown-HA-webinar/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-s-upgrade-breaks-reasoning-barriers" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Stop wasting 95% of your data labeling budget</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://link.voxel51.com/the-rundown-HA-webinar/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-s-upgrade-breaks-reasoning-barriers" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/6be0cd36-a45a-4a01-8617-9710f98d4cf0/image2__15_.jpg?t=1770920050"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> Most teams are labeling massive amounts of data that never gets used for model training. Voxel51&#39;s technical workshop on Feb. 18 shows how to build feedback-driven annotation pipelines that eliminate over-labeling — saving time and money while improving model performance.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Join the workshop and learn:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">How to use zero-shot selection and embeddings for maximum cost savings</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">QA workflows to review specific objects and fix errors fast</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">How to implement dedicated test sets to catch label drift early</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Debugging with embeddings to visualize the clusters confusing your model</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://link.voxel51.com/the-rundown-HA-webinar/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-s-upgrade-breaks-reasoning-barriers" target="_blank" rel="noopener style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">OPENAI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">⚡ <b><a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/introducing-gpt-5-3-codex-spark/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-s-upgrade-breaks-reasoning-barriers" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">OAI launches ultra-fast coding model on Cerebras chips</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/01c06635-6f08-4883-b15f-c560725c6f28/spark-codex.jpg?t=1770926178"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: OpenAI</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>OpenAI <a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/introducing-gpt-5-3-codex-spark/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-s-upgrade-breaks-reasoning-barriers" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">released</a> GPT-5.3-Codex-Spark, a new speed-optimized coding model that runs on Cerebras hardware, cranking out 1,000+ tokens per second and marking the company&#39;s first AI product powered by chips beyond its Nvidia stack.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Spark trades intelligence for speed, trailing the full 5.3-Codex on SWE-Bench Pro and Terminal-Bench but finishing tasks in a fraction of the time.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The release comes just weeks after OAI inked a $10B+ deal with Cerebras and separate agreements with AMD and Broadcom, diversifying away from Nvidia. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OAI&#39;s vision is for Spark to handle quick interactive edits while the full Codex tackles longer autonomous tasks in the background.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The model is rolling out as a research preview for ChatGPT Pro subs, with API access initially limited to a handful of enterprise design partners.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Codex&#39;s main criticism has been its speed, and OpenAI just addressed it in a big way — while making its chip diversification play real with the first product built on Cerebras hardware. Real-time coding with instant feedback will definitely change workflows for development tasks that are able to compromise a bit of power for speed.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">📺 <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/how-to-generate-a-tv-commercial-with-ai?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-s-upgrade-breaks-reasoning-barriers" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">How to generate a TV commercial with AI</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/9d84e280-68ef-43e1-a893-b10dec7674c9/Gemini_Generated_Image_j7e35cj7e35cj7e3.png?t=1770933696"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you will learn to generate a 20-second ad in the style of a professional TV commercial — taking the guesswork out of outputs without needing to click and pray.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Think of a commercial idea and ask Gemini to plan out two 5s scenes. Once done, ask it to write prompts for the start and end frames of both scenes. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Now, log in to <a class="link" href="https://Higgsfield.ai?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-s-upgrade-breaks-reasoning-barriers" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Higgsfield</a> (you will need a basic/pro plan) and click Image &gt; Create Image &gt; Nano Banana Pro. Set 4k quality, 4 variations, and 21:9 ratio.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Generate the start + end frame for scene 1 and just the end frame for scene 2. Download the ones you like best.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">In Higgsfield, go to Video &gt; Kling 3.0, upload your frames with the short scene prompt, and hit generate. After this, stitch the videos in a free editor.</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> Ask Gemini to use photography terms like “Hero shot” when generating scene prompts. You can also generate music for the ad with Suno + Eleven Labs.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PRESENTED BY CDATA</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;"><span style="font-family:"Apple Color Emoji", "Segoe UI Emoji", "Segoe UI Symbol";font-size:1em;">🏗️</span> <span style="color:inherit;"><b><a class="link" href="https://www.cdata.com/resources/workshop-build-copilot-agent-with-microsoft/?utm_source=rundown&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=26Q1_Microsoft_Copilot_Webinar" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Build secure agentic AI that scales</span></a></b></span></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://www.cdata.com/resources/workshop-build-copilot-agent-with-microsoft/?utm_source=rundown&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=26Q1_Microsoft_Copilot_Webinar" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/2ac2871f-52d6-4150-ba8e-06e364d22373/image1__46_.png?t=1770920131"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> Microsoft and CData are teaming up for a live 45-minute session on how to design secure, scalable agentic infrastructure using Copilot Studio, Agent 365, and CData&#39;s Connect AI — including a live cross-system workflow demo.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>In this session, you&#39;ll learn:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">How Microsoft and CData deliver connectivity, context, and control for production AI agents</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Agent design and production best practices from both teams</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">How a Copilot Studio agent syncing with Salesforce and Dynamics 365 is built and deployed</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://www.cdata.com/resources/workshop-build-copilot-agent-with-microsoft/?utm_source=rundown&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=26Q1_Microsoft_Copilot_Webinar" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Register here for the session</a></span>. All registrants will receive the session recording.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">MINIMAX</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;"><b>💰 </b><a class="link" href="https://www.minimax.io/news/minimax-m25?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-s-upgrade-breaks-reasoning-barriers" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b>MiniMax&#39;s open-source M2.5 hits frontier coding levels</b></span></a></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/7ed4cb1b-9a7c-4db4-9ba3-a1c2dab2f903/minimax25.jpg?t=1770934024"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: MiniMax</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Chinese AI lab MiniMax <a class="link" href="https://www.minimax.io/news/minimax-m25?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-s-upgrade-breaks-reasoning-barriers" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">launched</a> M2.5, an open-source model that rivals Opus 4.6 and GPT-5 on agentic coding benchmarks — but at a fraction of the cost, making it cheap enough to power AI agents running around the clock. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">M2.5 shows especially strong coding performance, scoring roughly even with Opus 4.6 and GPT-5.2 across key development benchmarks.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Two APIs are available: a faster M2.5-Lightning ($2.40/M output) and a standard M2.5 ($1.20/M output), both priced much lower than Opus ($25/M). </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">MiniMax revealed that M2.5 now handles 30% of daily company tasks across R&D, product, sales, HR, and finance, as well as 80% of new code commits.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The models are available via API, though the open-source weights and license have yet to be published. </p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Every few months, it feels like a Chinese lab drops a model that changes the cost math for the entire industry. M2.5’s frontier-level coding at this price makes &quot;intelligence too cheap to meter&quot; feel closer than ever, an important development as agents handling longer autonomous tasks become more common.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:center;"><span style="color:#FFFFFF;"><b>QUICK HITS</b></span></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h3 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🛠️ <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://www.rundown.ai/tools?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-s-upgrade-breaks-reasoning-barriers" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Trending AI Tools</a></b></span></h3><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">🔒 <a class="link" href="https://deal.incogni.io/aff_c?offer_id=6&aff_id=1889&url_id=1&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=google-s-upgrade-breaks-reasoning-barriers" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><b>Incogni</b></a> - remove your personal data from the web so scammers and identity thieves can’t access it. nofollow">hosted</a> its first all-hands since merging with SpaceX, with CEO Elon Musk outlining a major reorganization, product roadmap updates, and lunar ambitions, all aimed at outpacing rivals and taking xAI to the forefront of AI.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Musk acknowledged the <a class="link" href="https://www.rundown.ai/articles/xai-co-founder-exodus-continues?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-next-phase-unleashed" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">departure</a> of team members and outlined a new structure for xAI, saying the move was meant to be “more effective” at scale.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The new <a class="link" href="https://x.com/MarioNawfal/status/2021695841077981664?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-next-phase-unleashed" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">structure</a> has four core teams: Grok (chat and voice), a coding-focused unit, the Imagine team, and Macrohard (agents emulating companies).</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">He also <a class="link" href="https://x.com/XFreeze/status/2021685109796036787?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-next-phase-unleashed" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">spoke</a> about future infrastructure plans with SpaceX, including setting up AI satellite factories on the Moon — using lunar resources and solar energy.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Musk added that SpaceX will also build an electromagnetic mass driver to “shoot” AI satellites/components for massive deep space data centers.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Musk is no stranger to audacious promises, and his timelines often shift. But by broadcasting xAI’s tightened focus, product roadmap, and ambitious lunar plans, he’s making sure the world knows he’s aiming to build advanced AI in a way no other AI giant is — scaling beyond Earth’s resource limits instead of draining them.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">TOGETHER WITH MODULATE</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🗣️ <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://preview.modulate.ai/?utm_source=therundown&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=elmlaunch" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Voice-native AI architecture is here</a></b></span></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://preview.modulate.ai/?utm_source=therundown&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=elmlaunch" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/0e6de1fc-e98c-47a3-b949-e04f349b8065/image1.png?t=1770864280"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> Voice-specialized AI is here, and unlike OpenAI, xAI, and other leaders, it understands conversations and meaning — not just transcripts. Velma 2.0 is the world’s first voice-native AI designed to provide human-level, real-time conversation intelligence.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>By orchestrating 100+ sub-models purpose-built for voice, Velma allows you to:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Decode intent, emotion, stress, and authenticity in messy, multilingual audio</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Analyze audio 100x faster, cheaper, and more accurately than with LLMs</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Get traceable outputs with an explainable path</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://preview.modulate.ai/?utm_source=therundown&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=elmlaunch" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Try Velma</a></span> for yourself to understand the true meaning of your conversations.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">Z.AI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🧠 <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://z.ai/blog/glm-5?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-next-phase-unleashed" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Z.ai’s GLM-5 — the new open-source king</a></b></span></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/5c7898d9-38b1-439d-bbd4-61f170e862d4/HA5wnbCaMAAsTda__1_.jpeg?t=1770878153"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Artificial Analysis</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>China’s <a class="link" href="http://Z.ai?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-next-phase-unleashed" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Z.ai</a> just <a class="link" href="https://z.ai/blog/glm-5?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-next-phase-unleashed" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">launched</a> GLM-5, a 744B-parameter open-weights model that further closes the gap with the West’s frontier — sitting just behind Claude Opus 4.6 and GPT-5.2 on Artificial Analysis benchmarks.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">GLM-5 scored 50 on Artificial Analysis’ Intelligence Index, surpassing closed models like Gemini 3 Pro and Grok 4 as well as open-source ones like Kimi K2.5.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The model uses DeepSeek’s Sparse Attention architecture with just 40B active parameters, and runs inference on Chinese chips, including Huawei Ascend.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">On Humanity’s Last Exam, it hit 50.4 with tools, beating Opus 4.5, Gemini 3 Pro, and GPT-5.2. The coding performance on SWE-Bench was also close.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">GLM-5 is open-source under an MIT license, available now on HuggingFace, <a class="link" href="https://Z.ai?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-next-phase-unleashed" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Z.ai</a>’s own platform, and via API at $1 per million input tokens.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>The wave of Seedance 2.0’s viral AI clips hasn’t even faded, and there we have another near-frontier model from China that is already knocking at the door. The gap with the West isn’t closed yet, but with open weights, competitive pricing, and domestic chip support, it’s definitely narrowing faster than ever.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🎥 <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/turn-sop-training-documents-into-talking-head-training-videos?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-next-phase-unleashed" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Turn SOP docs into talking-head training videos</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/96e0274d-b99a-47d4-befe-e1ff9e5c1400/CleanShot_2026-02-11_at_16.49.29_2x.png?t=1770865085"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you will learn how to turn boring onboarding docs into engaging training videos narrated by an AI avatar. We tried a lot of tools and found the most efficient system for building quality AI training videos in bulk.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Take your training doc and prompt Claude/ChatGPT with &quot;Turn this into a three-minute training video script for an AI-generated avatar. Only include text overlays with bullets. The avatar can be seated, standing, head-on, etc.&quot;</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Save the script as a text file and go to <a class="link" href="https://Synthesia.io?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-next-phase-unleashed" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Synthesia.io</a> &gt; Create New Video &gt; Create from AI &gt; Upload the script file, with objective and audience description</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Choose a template and click Create Outline<b>.</b> Review the outline and follow the steps to generate your video. It should take 10-25 minutes to generate</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">When the video is complete, you can download and embed it somewhere like Notion or Google Docs</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip: </b>Repeat this for all onboarding docs to set up one-page onboarding that can be handed to any trainee!</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Anthropic details Claude Opus 4.6’s sabotage risk</a></b></span></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Nano Banana / The Rundown</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Anthropic <a class="link" href="https://www-cdn.anthropic.com/f21d93f21602ead5cdbecb8c8e1c765759d9e232.pdf?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-next-phase-unleashed" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">published</a> its latest Sabotage Risk Report, revealing that its new Claude Opus 4.6 model displays an “elevated susceptibility” to be misused for “heinous crimes,” including assisting in the development of chemical weapons.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Anthropic found Opus 4.6 knowingly supported crimes like chemical weapon development in small ways, but could not execute attacks on its own.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">When tasked to achieve a specific goal in a multi-agent test, the model proved far more willing to manipulate and deceive other agents than previous models.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Considering these findings, Anthropic deemed the overall sabotage risk “very low but not negligible” due to the model’s lack of coherent misaligned goals.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The company also classified the model’s capabilities as entering a “gray zone” that necessitated this mandatory report under its Responsible Scaling Policy.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Anthropic’s CEO Dario Amodei recently <a class="link" href="https://www.therundown.ai/p/anthropic-ceo-confronts-ais-dangers?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-next-phase-unleashed" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">highlighted</a> the risks of advanced AI, and now, one of his own models appears to be moving into the gray zone. With growing competition from OpenAI, Google, xAI, and Chinese labs, the pressure to push capabilities forward may only intensify the very risks he has warned about.</p></div><p class="paragraph" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Community AI workflows</a></b></span></h3><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Every newsletter, we showcase how a reader is using AI to work smarter, save time, or make life easier.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Today’s workflow comes from reader <b>Lindsay F.</b> in Kingsville, Ontario:</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">“I own a 1970 Chevelle SS and am converting it into a modern driving ‘restomod.’ I am using both ChatGPT & Copilot to research and develop the entire restoration plan. The restoration of the vehicle will take place in phases, and the agents have provided me with a priority list, options for what parts to purchase, and where to source them from. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">They have also developed a budget for the project, including parts & local labor rates and what the finished project will look like upon completion. I am 72 years old and just love how much this is helping me.”</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">How do you use AI? Tell us <a class="link" href="https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSfH4UPzu72HTpdb08Qlm-0dLwKJIjdcAwCcAvVywcHD6mwKig/viewform?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-next-phase-unleashed" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">here</a>.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section"
