style="text-align:left;">XAI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🚪 <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://x.com/Yuhu_ai_/status/2021113745024614671?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">xAI&#39;s co-founder exodus continues</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/58ba38bd-404c-4007-af4b-ac06e7d0ee7f/tonywu.jpg?t=1770747848"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Tony Wu (@Yuhu_ai_ on X)</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>xAI co-founders, Tony Wu and Jimmy Ba, just <a class="link" href="https://x.com/Yuhu_ai_/status/2021113745024614671?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">announced</a> their departures from Elon Musk&#39;s AI startup, making them the fourth and fifth founding members to walk away from the company, coming right after its SpaceX mega-merger. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Wu <a class="link" href="https://x.com/Yuhu_ai_/status/2021113745024614671?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">posted</a> on X that it’s “time for my next chapter”, saying a “small team armed with AIs can move mountains and redefine what’s possible”. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Wu led Grok&#39;s reasoning efforts and reported directly to Musk, joining xAI from Google in 2023, with no reason given for his departure. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Ba <a class="link" href="https://x.com/jimmybajimmyba/status/2021374875793801447?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">announced</a> his departure late Tuesday, saying that 2026 will be the “busiest and most consequential year for the future of our species.”</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Musk had <a class="link" href="https://www.theinformation.com/articles/inside-musks-spacex-xai-megamerger?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">reportedly</a> &quot;grown frustrated&quot; with delays to new Grok models in recent weeks, with its anticipated 4.20 update still awaiting release.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>xAI has a SpaceX merger in motion, accelerating model competition, deepfake blowback, and now a wave of senior exits is a lot of fires for a startup whose ambitions just jumped to space-based data centers. If there is anyone used to juggling chaotic situations, it’s Elon — but this leadership exodus is starting to raise questions. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">TOGETHER WITH LAMBDA</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🧠 <b><a class="link" href="https://lambda.ai/blog/2025-ai-wrapped?utm_source=rundown-ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=2026-01-2025-wrapped-blog&utm_content=secondary-ad-feb-11" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">2025 in AI, insights from hundreds of deployments</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://lambda.ai/blog/2025-ai-wrapped?utm_source=rundown-ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=2026-01-2025-wrapped-blog&utm_content=secondary-ad-feb-11" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/cdc87d99-cca6-4b9a-bdf9-f4d0bfeb7ab4/image3__25_.png?t=1770748087"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> AI changed meaningfully in 2025, not just in research, but in production. Lambda’s 2025 AI wrapped breaks down the shifts that defined the year, from reasoning models and larger context windows to multimodal capabilities, open-source viability, and inference-first workloads.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Key shifts covered:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Reasoning, long-context, and multimodal models</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Open-source and MoE-driven efficiency gains</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Inference overtaking training in production</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://lambda.ai/blog/2025-ai-wrapped?utm_source=rundown-ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=2026-01-2025-wrapped-blog&utm_content=secondary-ad-feb-11" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Read the report</a></span>.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">ENTIRE</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">💰 <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://entire.io/blog/hello-entire-world?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Ex-GitHub CEO&#39;s startup lands $60M</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/e1ca3ddc-f479-4e01-beba-d57b5ed81949/entire-github.jpg?t=1770760369"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Entire</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Ex-GitHub CEO Thomas Dohmke <a class="link" href="https://entire.io/blog/hello-entire-world?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">raised</a> a record $60M seed round for Entire, an open-source developer platform designed to track and manage AI-generated code that is increasingly being shipped without humans reading it themselves.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Dohmke <a class="link" href="https://x.com/ashtom/status/1954920157853172064?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">left</a> Microsoft-owned GitHub last August after four years, saying the dev tools he built weren&#39;t made for a world where agents write the code.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Entire’s first release is Checkpoints, which logs AI agent actions like prompts and decisions while coding, so devs can better audit the outputs.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The tool works with both Claude Code and Gemini CLI, with OpenAI’s Codex and GitHub support coming soon. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The $60M seed round is the largest ever for a dev tools startup, putting the company’s initial valuation at $300M at launch. </p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Dohmke helped lead the platform where most of the world’s code lives, and him now building the agentic tooling layer is a strong signal of where the industry is heading. As AI generates more code than humans can review, helping devs trust and manage the output could be just as important as the agents themselves.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🔎<a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/how-this-hidden-insights-feature-improves-claude-code?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"> </a><b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/how-this-hidden-insights-feature-improves-claude-code?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Improve Claude Code with “Insights” feature</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/b51e7daa-7cda-42d5-bdd6-6ef314c09ddb/audit.jpg?t=1770760829"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you will learn how to use the Claude Code’s “insights” feature to improve your coding habits. This hidden, built-in report gives you feedback directly from Claude Code, and will even build you custom skills and agent instructions.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Open a new terminal session. Run the command <code>claude /insights</code>.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Claude should begin working on your insights report. When it’s done, it will give you a link to a file named <code>report.html</code>. Copy it into an empty folder.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Open your code editor (we use Cursor). Start the webpage with <code>cmd + shift + p</code> and find the “Open <a class="link" href="https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=ritwickdey.LiveServer&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Live Server</a>” tool.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">You’ll see the report outlining what worked, what didn’t, and how to improve. Use the “Existing CC Features to Try” section for new project instructions.</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> You can also give the HTML to Claude/ChatGPT and have the assistant run it. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PRESENTED BY GLEAN</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🤝 <b><a class="link" href="https://www.glean.com/glean-live/?utm_source=3rd-party&utm_medium=email&utm_campaign=glean-live-feb-17&utm_partner=rundown&utm_content=Feb-11" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Meet your new AI work partner</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://www.glean.com/glean-live/?utm_source=3rd-party&utm_medium=email&utm_campaign=glean-live-feb-17&utm_partner=rundown&utm_content=Feb-11" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/b0886930-c062-45d3-927e-aca2f76089bf/image1__17_.jpg?t=1770748195"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> Join Glean’s flagship virtual launch event to discover their latest-gen AI assistant: an enterprise‑ready AI work partner that actually helps people get things done. Hear from speakers at Glean, Swiggy, and more, and learn how leading teams are turning enterprise context into real business impact.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Register for Glean:LIVE on Feb. 17 to:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Learn how context-aware AI drives broad adoption and lasting impact</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" Assistant — personalized, proactive, and a true domain expert</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://www.glean.com/glean-live/?utm_source=3rd-party&utm_medium=email&utm_campaign=glean-live-feb-17&utm_partner=rundown&utm_content=Feb-11" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Register now</a></span> to save your spot for Glean:LIVE.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI RESEARCH</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">⏳ <b><a class="link" href="https://hbr.org/2026/02/ai-doesnt-reduce-work-it-intensifies-it?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Harvard finds AI tools expand workloads</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/ceff5f3c-7b98-49ee-8fc9-d66284ca22fe/overload.jpg?t=1770760851"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Lovart / The Rundown</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>A new Harvard Business Review research <a class="link" href="https://hbr.org/2026/02/ai-doesnt-reduce-work-it-intensifies-it?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">found</a> that AI tools at a U.S. tech company didn&#39;t lighten employee workloads over 8 months, but actually grew them, with workers taking on broader tasks, logging more hours, and multitasking more.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The study tracked ~200 employees who adopted AI on their own, observing work habits and conducting 40+ in-depth interviews over eight months. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Workers utilizing AI expanded well beyond their roles, with the tech making unfamiliar work feel doable.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The study also noted AI blurring lines between work and rest, with employees firing off prompts after hours or during breaks.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Engineers also reported spending more time reviewing and coaching colleagues on AI-assisted code, with &quot;vibe-coding&quot; help requests piling up.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>AI was supposed to free workers up, not quietly pile more on their plates — but that&#39;s exactly what Harvard found happening. The tech’s productivity gains are real, but so is the tradeoff of broader roles, blurred boundaries, and a new work pace that is changing more quickly than many employees are likely ready for.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:center;"><span style="color:#FFFFFF;"><b>QUICK HITS</b></span></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h3 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🛠️ <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://www.rundown.ai/tools?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Trending AI Tools</a></b></span></h3><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">🤖<b> </b><a class="link" href="https://www.warp.dev/oz?utm_source=publications&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=oz_launch_02_11_multiple&utm_content=the_rundown" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Oz from Warp</a> – Launch hundreds of cloud agents in minutes, from Warp, API, or integrations. target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Community AI workflows</a></b></span></h3><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Every newsletter, we showcase how a reader is using AI to work smarter, save time, or make life easier.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Today’s workflow comes from reader <b>Devin P.</b> in Talladega, AL:</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">&quot;I&#39;m a blind person, so I use screen readers to use computers and phones. Even though the Android apps for a lot of AI apps could be more accessible to me, the CLI coding packages, like Codex and Gemini CLI, are pretty nice. I first used Gemini to make Termux, a Linux Terminal app for Android, more accessible, resulting in <a class="link" href="https://github.com/devinprater/Talking-termux-app?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=xai-s-co-founder-exodus-continues" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Talking Termux</a>.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">I then had AI set up Emacs with a speech system called Emacspeak, dealing with Termux&#39;s differences to Linux, and the lack of a TCLX package. ByteDance is <a class="link" surpass current top available systems. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details:</b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The model can reportedly handle text, image, audio, and video inputs, with tests showing impressive outputs across a range of styles and use cases.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The system also features native audio generation, 2K resolution, and 15s outputs, currently only available via ByteDance’s Jimeng AI video platform.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">ByteDance also class="heading" style="text-align:left;">TOGETHER WITH MONGODB</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">📈<b> </b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" prototype to production, faster</b></a></span></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" information from thousands of interactions, and connect AI agents to their data without custom plumbing.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>With MongoDB&#39;s platform, you 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">OPENAI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">📢 <b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/testing-ads-in-chatgpt/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=bytedance-stuns-the-ai-video-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">OpenAI officially starts showing ads in ChatGPT</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/57c3621e-6e97-4b03-a811-c61de5e3dd8e/adschatgpt.jpg?t=1770676862"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: OpenAI</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>OpenAI just officially started <a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/testing-ads-in-chatgpt/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=bytedance-stuns-the-ai-video-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">testing</a> ads in ChatGPT for U.S. users on its free and $8/month Go tiers, a move the company has been circling for months and that Anthropic used as ammo for its Super Bowl ad campaign this past weekend. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Ads appear below chat responses and are targeted based on the active conversation, chat history, memory, and prior ad engagement.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">OAI emphasized that the ad content will not impact ChatGPT’s answers, “protecting the trust (users) place in it for important and personal tasks”. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Free-tier users can opt out of advertising entirely, but doing so cuts their daily message allowance — acting as a funnel towards paid plans. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The pilot has a reported minimum price tag of $200K for advertisers, with major marketing firms like Omnicom already <a class="link" href="https://www.adweek.com/media/chatgpt-gets-ads-omnicom-wpp-and-dentsu-line-up-brands-for-openai-pilot/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=bytedance-stuns-the-ai-video-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">locking in</a> spots for their clients. </p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>We’ve frequently said ads within AI feels like a slippery slope, but OAI is ripping the band-aid as the first test case for the industry. While the execution seems fine, encroaching sponsors could change the dynamic of how many experience ChatGPT — still, the tradeoff for free access to advanced intelligence is hard to argue. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">📞<a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/build-this-ai-powered-sales-objection-handler?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=bytedance-stuns-the-ai-video-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" style="color: inherit"> </a><b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/build-this-ai-powered-sales-objection-handler?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=bytedance-stuns-the-ai-video-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Build an AI-powered sales objection handler</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/b89244c8-896f-4e03-be1c-082edcb2f9dd/image_-_2026-02-09T135713.539.png?t=1770667057"/></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you will learn how to actually build something useful with those sales call transcripts you are accumulating. This is a simple, weekly process that turns your weekly call transcripts into a handy, quick reference document.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Create a ChatGPT Project named &quot;Sales Objections&quot;. Upload a text file listing your product lines, pricing, and core offers so the AI understands what you sell.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Go to Instructions in project settings and paste: &quot;Read the attached transcripts. Create a weekly report template. For every objection: Number the objection, State the objection clearly, Provide 3 descriptive bullets on the context, List which lead or prospect surfaced it, Provide two short, punchy rebuttals.”</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Each week, upload call transcripts into your project. Make sure they have the date and name of the client. Open a new thread, and tell it to create the report.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Open a blank Notion page. Create a “Toggle Heading” for the week (e.g., &quot;Week of Feb 9&quot;). Copy the ChatGPT output and paste it inside the toggle.</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> Connect Notion inside ChatGPT (Settings → Connected Apps) so ChatGPT can see your current page and reference past weeks.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PRESENTED BY TELY AI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🔎<b> </b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://www.tely.ai/?utm_source=newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_campaign=rundown-jul-25" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><b>Are you invisible in AI search?</b></a></span></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://www.tely.ai/?utm_source=newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_campaign=rundown-jul-25" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/ba7c483f-e4dc-4a4b-af3a-4f27eda8cd0f/image2__43_.png?t=1770658446"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> You’re in a niche industry. style="text-align:left;">SELF-DRIVING CARS & AI</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🚗 <b><a class="link" href="https://waymo.com/blog/2026/02/the-waymo-world-model-a-new-frontier-for-autonomous-driving-simulation?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=bytedance-stuns-the-ai-video-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Waymo taps Genie 3 to train self-driving cars</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/a6de9635-cb17-4942-92f2-f2648a9b74aa/waymomodel.jpg?t=1770674751"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: Waymo</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Waymo just <a class="link" href="https://waymo.com/blog/2026/02/the-waymo-world-model-a-new-frontier-for-autonomous-driving-simulation?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=bytedance-stuns-the-ai-video-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">introduced</a> the Waymo World Model, a driving simulator built on DeepMind&#39;s Genie 3 that generates hyper-realistic scenarios the company&#39;s fleet of self-driving cars has never encountered to help it deal with extreme edge cases.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The model takes Genie 3&#39;s visual knowledge and converts it into paired camera and lidar outputs, helping dream up scenarios its cars have never actually seen.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Engineers can reshape scenes with text prompts, driving inputs, or layout edits (like changing weather or adding obstacles) to test &quot;what if&quot; responses.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Waymo found a workaround for Genie 3&#39;s short memory by running footage at 4x speed, stretching simulations long enough to cover longer driving tasks.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Google&#39;s Street View data gave Waymo a head start in mapping the real world for its cars, but world models can now generate the extreme edge cases that no amount of road miles can produce. Waymo’s use of Genie is a prime example of one of the top use cases for world models — simulations for robotics training data.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:center;"><span style="color:#FFFFFF;"><b>COMMUNITY</b></span></p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h3 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🤝 <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><b><a class="link" href="https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSfH4UPzu72HTpdb08Qlm-0dLwKJIjdcAwCcAvVywcHD6mwKig/viewform?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=bytedance-stuns-the-ai-video-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Community AI workflows</a></b></span></h3><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Every newsletter, we showcase how a reader is using AI to work smarter, save time, or make life easier.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Today’s workflow comes from reader <b>Clay D.</b> in Carson City, NV:</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">&quot;After serving in combat in Iraq, I was initially rated at 50% disabled by the VA. I knew that rating did not fully reflect the severity of my conditions...</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">I provided ChatGPT with my medical records, original claim, and publicly available VA Board of Veterans’ Appeals decisions from other similar cases. I instructed it to identify approval and denial patterns, apply relevant claim law, and rewrite my claim to avoid errors. The result was a stronger submission that led to a 100% VA disability rating...&quot;</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">How do you use AI? Tell us <a class="link" href="https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSfH4UPzu72HTpdb08Qlm-0dLwKJIjdcAwCcAvVywcHD6mwKig/viewform?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=bytedance-stuns-the-ai-video-world" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">here</a>.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> RAG was step one—but retrieval alone doesn&#39;t guarantee accuracy. <a class="link" href="https://you.com/resources/what-is-ai-grounding-downloadable?utm_campaign=32665437-Rundown_Q1&utm_source=external-newsletter&utm_medium=email&utm_term=rundown_primary_2.9.26&utm_content=rundown_primary_2.9.26" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">THE RUNDOWN ROUNDTABLE</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">💡<b><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a class="link" href="https://www.rundown.ai?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-ads-steal-the-show-at-super-bowl-lx" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">The Rundown Roundtable: Our AI use cases</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/fcff2576-00e6-47f2-b965-3b87eb2719f5/roundtable.jpg?t=1769962029"/><div class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image Source: Ideogram / The Rundown</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>The Rundown Roundtable is a weekly feature in which we poll members of The Rundown staff about how we use AI in our work and daily lives.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Jennifer, Tech & Robotics Writer: </b>I put Gemini Deep Research and Perplexity Pro to work as my personal research assistants. For robotics research, I tell them to stick to top-tier journals and primary sources only, and demand citations and dates for everything. Then I have them distill the highlights into a ranked list so I know exactly where to dig deeper.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Billy, University Educator: </b>Every Sunday night, my Openclaw asks me to recap my week and send it some photos I took. It makes a collage of the photos and generates a stylized “magazine cover” based on the recap. At the end of the year, I should have a neat collection of time capsules.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Jason, Developer: </b>I&#39;ve been taking topics I want to learn about (mostly coding docs for new technologies) and giving them to NotebookLM to create customized podcasts for my runs when there aren&#39;t interesting podcasts available from the channels I frequent. And it really is actually good and enjoyable, and not just AI slop. </p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">AI TRAINING</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🧑‍💻 <b><a class="link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/how-to-build-a-lead-magnet-tool-for-your-website-with-replit?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-ads-steal-the-show-at-super-bowl-lx" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Build lead widgets for your site without coding</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><a class="image__link" href="https://app.therundown.ai/guides/how-to-build-a-lead-magnet-tool-for-your-website-with-replit?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-ads-steal-the-show-at-super-bowl-lx" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" src="https://media.beehiiv.com/cdn-cgi/image/fit=scale-down,format=auto,onerror=redirect,quality=80/uploads/asset/file/ca391d8a-7dce-4a0f-81b4-6e214148dcbb/image_-_2026-02-08T100528.294.png?t=1770566762"/></a></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you will learn how to use Replit to build a custom calculator lead form for your website. If you can copy and paste, you can build software for your team, and you’ll save on per-seat pricing.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Go to <b><a class="link" href="https://Replit.com?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-ads-steal-the-show-at-super-bowl-lx" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Replit</a></b>, toggle on &quot;Plan mode,&quot; and prompt: &quot;Build a custom lead gen widget app using Python (Flask) and Replit SQL. Users will create embeddable cost-savings calculators that capture email leads and track analytics. Allow custom colors, form fields and formulas.&quot; </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Answer any follow-ups from the agent and hit “Build” when ready. Once it finishes, test the tool in the preview tab. Try creating a new lead widget.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Copy the widget’s embed (iframe) code and embed it on your brand website, then check captured leads in Replit → Database → Development Database.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">If everything works, click “Publish”. Replit will deploy your app to a public URL. You will need to log in to this version and re-create your form.</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> Use this method to embed anything on your site — a slideshow, countdown timer, or even a blog.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#FFFFFF;border-color:#000000;border-radius:10px;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;"><h6 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">PRESENTED BY GITLAB</h6><h4 class="heading" style="text-align:left;">🤖<b> </b><a class="link" class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: <a class="link" nofollow">ai.com</a></p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>Crypto.com co-founder and CEO Kris Marszalek <a class="link" href="https://ai.com/company-news/ai-com-launch?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-ads-steal-the-show-at-super-bowl-lx" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">revealed</a> he purchased the AI.com domain for $70M, the largest domain sale ever, debuting the site as an autonomous AI agent platform for consumers with a Super Bowl commercial. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The platform promises a personal AI agent that can trade stocks, manage calendars, send messages, and automate workflows with no technical setup.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">The record-breaking deal nearly doubled the prior domain record set by <a class="link" href="https://voice.com?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=ai-ads-steal-the-show-at-super-bowl-lx" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">voice.com</a>&#39;s $30M sale in 2019. </p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Marszalek envisions a network of agents that autonomously build new capabilities and share upgrades across users, “accelerating the advent of AGI”. </p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>That’s certainly one way to make a big splash — with both the largest domain sale ever (admittedly for an excellent one) and a primetime entrance with a Super Bowl ad. But a strong marketing play and a tool that actually competes with the flurry of agentic upgrades from established, frontier labs are two very different beasts. </p></div><p class="paragraph" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Cut down reporting times with Claude in Excel</a></span></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown:</b> In this guide, you will do a quick exercise that teaches you how to use Claude as a spreadsheet architect, taking 5+ messy CSVs and watching Claude handle data cleaning, table formatting, color-coding, and more.<br><br><b>Step-by-step:</b></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Install Claude’s Excel app from the <a class="link" href="https://marketplace.microsoft.com/en-us/product/saas/wa200009404?tab=overview&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-anthropic-fight-on-the-frontier" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">Microsoft Marketplace</a>. For this example, we used a year’s worth of SEO data, but you can use sales data, receipts, etc</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">In Excel, click the Claude button and prompt “I have [data type] data from [sources] for my website/brand/team. Make a plan to rename each tab and clean the data up to make it more readable”. Then, edit and approve the plan</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Once done, ask Claude to make a plan for the master dashboard tab: “Based on all tabs, what’s the best way to tie this data into a Master Dashboard?”</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Finally, you can ask Claude to visualize data with prompts like <i>“</i>Create a combo chart for Clicks vs. Average Position”</p></li></ol><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Pro tip:</b> Asking Claude to review the data and create a plan improves its output significantly compared to asking it to get started immediately.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" noreferrer nofollow"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">OpenAI’s Frontier to manage ‘AI coworkers’</span></a></b></h4><div class="image"><img alt="" class="image__image" style="border-radius:0px 0px 0px 0px;border-style:solid;border-width:0px 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;border-color:#E5E7EB;" class="image__source"><span class="image__source_text"><p>Image source: OpenAI</p></span></div></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The Rundown: </b>OpenAI just <a class="link" href="https://openai.com/index/introducing-openai-frontier/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-anthropic-fight-on-the-frontier" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">launched</a> Frontier, a new platform for enterprises to deploy and manage AI agents like new hires — complete with onboarding, permissions, and performance reviews across a company’s existing tech stack.</p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>The details: </b></p><ul><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Frontier connects to existing enterprise systems like CRMs and ticketing tools, letting agents pull context from across the business without migrations.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Built-in eval and feedback loops let agents learn via experience, with OAI comparing it to onboarding a new employee with reviews and boundaries.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">Every agent operates under its own profile with scoped access and hard limits on what it can touch for enterprise and regulated control.</p></li><li><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;">HP, Oracle, State Farm, and Uber are among the first adopters, with OAI embedding engineers on-site to help teams get agents into production.</p></li></ul><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Why it matters: </b>Anthropic and OAI have been battling over models and coding tools, but Frontier shows the fight is also bleeding into who controls the enterprise agent layer underneath. Model capabilities are making AI coworkers a reality in the near future, and the system that ultimately orchestrates them will be valuable real estate. </p></div><p class="paragraph" </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Lotus Health </b><a class="link" noreferrer nofollow">raised</a> $35M in Series A funding for its free AI-powered primary care platform, providing diagnosis, prescriptions, and referrals across 50 states. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>Meta </b>is <a class="link" href="https://ai.meta.com/meta-ai/?utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-anthropic-fight-on-the-frontier" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">rolling out</a> a standalone app for its Vibes AI video platform, which was previously only available via the Meta app. </p><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"><b>AI evaluation firm METR</b> <a class="link" href="https://x.com/METR_Evals/status/2019169900317798857?s=20&utm_source=www.therundown.ai&utm_medium=newsletter&utm_campaign=openai-anthropic-fight-on-the-frontier" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">released</a> new analysis for GPT-5.2 (high), finding it can now handle tasks that would take a human engineer over 6 hours to complete.</p></div><p class="paragraph" style="text-align:left;"></p><div class="section" style="background-color:#000000;border-color:#000000;border-style:solid;border-width:2px;margin:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px 0.0px;padding:0.0px 0.0px 0.0px
